The Embedded Experts

Release notes for J-Link software and documentation package

Version V6.44h (2019-05-03)

  1. DLL: Autochips AC781x series devices, clock settings for flash module, fixed.
  2. DLL: Command string "CORESIGHT_SetMTBBufUsageSize" did not work correctly. (Only half of configured MTB buffer size was used) Fixed.
  3. DLL: Command string "CORESIGHT_SetMTBBufUseAddr" did not work correctly. Fixed.
  4. DLL: Improved sanity checks for MTB buffer configuration.
  5. DLL: Microchip (Atmel) ATSAM5x family: Under special circumstances, erase of the auxiliary space did not work. Fixed.
  6. DLL: Under certain circumstances connecting to a NXP Kinetis L Series device could fail. Introduced with V6.40. Fixed.
  7. DLL: Under special circumstances, the used timeout for Open Flashloader based algorithms was chosen too low resulting in timeout errors. Fixed.
  8. DLL: Under special circumstances, watchpoints got corrupted after single stepping. Fixed.
  9. GDBServer: Improved RTOS plugin for embOS to be more descriptive (info will be added to RTOS plugin SDK documentation as well)
  10. GDBServer: Improved RTOS plugin handling, especially when having FPU support
  11. J-Link SDK: J-Link Commander (Windows C sample) could not open files in the release configuration. Fixed.
  12. UM08001: Added missing - and updated existing command lines for all tools

Version V6.44g (2019-04-18)

  1. DLL: Extending existing devices through the JLinkDevices.xml from the hidden device database did not work. Fixed.
  2. DLL: ST STM32F412VG: Under special circumstances, flash programming did not work. Fixed.
  3. Flasher Firmware: Programming could fail, if the Flasher was not connected to a network or an USB host. Fixed.
  4. Flasher Firmware: Under special circumstances, flash programming of Open Flashloader based algorithms in stand-alone mode failed. Introduced in V6.44e. Fixed.

Version V6.44f (2019-04-12)

  1. AG: Firmware: J-Link-OB-K22-CortexM: Drag and drop programming could fail with "failed to allocate memory for buffer" FAIL.TXT. Fixed.
  2. AG: Installer (macOS): License text was outdated. Fixed.
  3. AG: DLL (Linux): Web Control Panel: Log tab did not work properly. Fixed.
  4. AG: DLL (macOS): Web Control Panel: Log tab did not work properly. Fixed.
  5. AG: SDK: JLINKARM_Core2CoreName() returned "RX" instead of "RX66T" when passing JLINK_CORE_RX66T. Fixed.
  6. AG: DLL: ST STM32H7 series: Improved flash programming speed.
  7. AG: DLL: When downloading to flash, empty sectors were erased again unnecessarily. (e.g. ST STM32H7 series) Fixed.
  8. AB: Flasher Firmware: Flasher Portable PLUS did not power off automatically after being charged. Fixed.
  9. AB: Flasher Firmware: Flasher Portable PLUS did not use the DisplayName tags. Fixed.

Version V6.44e (2019-04-05)

  1. Commander: "term" expected a capital letter as protocol selection for no reason. Fixed.
  2. DLL: Analog Devices ADuCM320: Under special circumstances, block verification errors could occur while an additional readback afterwards succeeded (data cache of flash controller was not invalidated correctly). Fixed.
  3. DLL: RISC-V: Latest Syntacore SCR1 bitstreams were no longer correctly detected as RISC-V cores. Fixed.
  4. DLL: Renesas S5D9 series: programming of option-setting memory did not work properly. Fixed.
  5. DLL: Reset did not work properly for LPC12xx series devices. Fixed.
  6. DLL: Some devices names passed by TI's Code Composer Studio (CCS) were not accepted by the J-Link DLL (e.g. TMS570LS20216SZWT). Fixed.
  7. DLL: Updated NXP's K32W device family support.
  8. Firmware Flashers: exit steps will only be executed after successful flashing
  9. Flasher ARM/PRO fixed missing CR LF after change baudrate command
  10. Package Linux: DEB/RPM package versioning was incorrect in case no patch level was applied (patch level == 0), so that for example V6.45 was considered older than V6.44a. Fixed.
  11. SDK: JLINKARM_GetDebugInfo(JLINKARM_DEBUG_INFO_HAS_FPU_INDEX) always returned -1 for ARM7/9 based devices. Fixed.

Version V6.44d (2019-03-27)

  1. Commander: Command "vtref" did not work correctly. Introduced in V6.42. Fixed.
  2. DLL: Added "RV64" as selection to list of supported devices
  3. DLL: ST STM32F4xx (Access line devices): Improved flash programming speed.
  4. DLL: ST STM32L0 family: Attach did not work. Fixed.
  5. DLL: Under special circumstances, target connection via JTAG did not work (e.g. for TI CC1310F128). Introduced in V6.44c. Fixed.
  6. GDBServer: Added support for RV64 (RISC-V 64-bit)
  7. GDBServer: Some cores were shown as ???. Fixed.
  8. J-Flash Lite: Some cores were shown as ???. Fixed.

Version V6.44c (2019-03-22)

  1. DLL (SDK): JLINKARM_JTAG_StoreInst() and JLINKARM_JTAG_StoreData() did not work correctly in case multiple devices where in the JTAG chain and a device was selected via JLINKARM_ConfigJTAG(). Fixed.
  2. DLL/J-Flash: The unlocking algorithm for STM32F0 series devices did not work correctly. Fixed.
  3. DLL: Added support for RV64 (RISC-V 64-bit)
  4. DLL: Flash programming support for Dialog Semiconductor DA14x95 series device, fixed.
  5. DLL: Microchip IS208x: Flash programming could fail if WDT on target device was already enabled. Fixed.
  6. DLL: Microchip IS208x: Halting core before first instruction of user code was executed at 0x20_0000 did not work properly. Fixed.
  7. DLL: SPIFI-Lib, restore of QE (Quad Enable) bit, fixed.
  8. DLL: ST STM32F4 Access Line (e.g. STM32F412VG): Flash programming did not work under special circumstances. Fixed.
  9. DLL: TI TMS570LS10 / TMS570LS10: Flash programming did not work. Fixed.
  10. Firmware: J-Link EDU/BASE/PLUS V10: Microchip IS208x 2-wire JTAG: Under very special circumstances, a response from the device was not evaluated correctly, leading to verify errors, even if everything was O.K. Fixed.
  11. Firmware: J-Link PRO V4: Microchip IS208x 2-wire JTAG: Under very special circumstances, a response from the device was not evaluated correctly, leading to verify errors, even if everything was O.K. Fixed.
  12. Firmware: J-Link ULTRA+ V4: Microchip IS208x 2-wire JTAG: Under very special circumstances, a response from the device was not evaluated correctly, leading to verify errors, even if everything was O.K. Fixed.
  13. J-Link Commander: RISC-V: Disassembly of LI instruction was disassembled incorrectly. Fixed.
  14. RTTViewer: Fixed RTT Control block addresses were not displayed inside the configuration dialog. Fixed.
  15. RTTViewer: Improved RTT data parsing speed.
  16. RTTViewer: Improved output speed of RTT data.
  17. RTTViewer: Terminals shared the same font color/ background color. Fixed.
  18. Software package (Windows): The uninstaller ignored the /S parameter. Fixed.

Version V6.44b (2019-03-15)

  1. DLL (Linux): DEB package tried to incorrectly remove symlink that pointed to the previously installed version. Fixed.
  2. DLL/Firmware Flasher: Option bytes programming could fail in stand-alone mode for Renesas S5D9 series devices. Fixed.
  3. DLL: Added command string "SetSkipDebugDeInit" to allow skipping of debug de-init at the end of a debug session. This may be used on Cortex-M for example to make sure that DEMCR.TRCENA stays enabled and so does the DWT unit and CYCCNT.
  4. DLL: Added device names for NXP iMXRT101x series devices, MIMXRT1015xxx4A, MIMXRT1015xxx5A.
  5. DLL: Added missing Cortex-A72 to device selection list.
  6. DLL: Microchip IS2083B: Changed halt address after reset to 0x27_0000
  7. DLL: NXP LPC51U68: "LPC51U68JBD48" and "LPC51U68JBD64" could not be selected as target device name. Fixed.
  8. DLL: NXP LPC8N804: Under special circumstances, reset did not work and returned an error. Fixed.
  9. DLL: NXP LPC8xx family: Some device names where not recognized by the J-Link DLL. Fixed.
  10. DLL: NXP i.MXRT1064: Flash programming support for the internal (QSPI) flash was not available for all iMXRT1064 devices. Fixed.
  11. DLL: NXP i.MXRT1064: Some devices names (e.g. MIMXRT1064xxx5A) were not recognized by the J-Link DLL. Fixed.
  12. Firmware Flasher: FTP server did not report errors for invalid paths. Fixed.
  13. J-Flash: J-Flash did not handle the alignment information for Open Flash Loader correctly. Fixed.
  14. J-Link CCS plugin: Added cJTAG support to the plugin / interface DLL.
  15. J-Link SDK: Documentation "SPI API" chapter: Added "SPI API Samples" section and corrected overextending line in "Indirect SPI API functions" section.

Version V6.44a (2019-03-08)

  1. DLL: Microchip IS208x series: Improved flash programming speed
  2. DLL: Microchip IS208x series: When debugging in Keil uVision, the error message "Cannot read register ACON while core is running" could occur. Fixed.
  3. DLL: Microchip PIC32MX family: For some devices (e.g. PIC32MX270F256D) unlock did not work. Fixed.
  4. DLL: NXP LPC55xx / LPC55SXX: Under special circumstances (flash erased), flash programming failed. Fixed.
  5. DLL: QSPI flash programming support for Freescale K80/K82 series devices, fixed.
  6. DLL: Updated unsecure dialog for Microchip PIC32xx series devices.
  7. Firmware (Flasher Portable PLUS): Added support for upt to 16 images
  8. Firmware (Flasher Portable PLUS): DisplayName corrected for Batch mode
  9. Firmware: J-Link EDU Mini: RISC-V: When writing memory via 32-bit system bus accesses, it could happen that garbage was written for the first 32-bit in case a 8-/16-bit access preceded the write. Fixed.
  10. Firmware: J-Link EDU/BASE/PLUS V10: RISC-V: When writing memory via 32-bit system bus accesses, it could happen that garbage was written for the first 32-bit in case a 8-/16-bit access preceded the write. Fixed.
  11. Firmware: J-Link PRO V4: RISC-V: When writing memory via 32-bit system bus accesses, it could happen that garbage was written for the first 32-bit in case a 8-/16-bit access preceded the write. Fixed.
  12. Firmware: J-Link ULTRA+ V4: RISC-V: When writing memory via 32-bit system bus accesses, it could happen that garbage was written for the first 32-bit in case a 8-/16-bit access preceded the write. Fixed.

Version V6.44 (2019-03-01)

  1. DLL Updater: Under some locale distributions of Windows, Keil uVision could not be updated. Fixed.
  2. DLL: Added Flash programming support for Autochip AC781x series devices.
  3. DLL: Added Flash programming support for Maxim MAX32625 and MAX32626 series devices.
  4. DLL: Added Flash programming support for STM32G070xx series devices.
  5. DLL: Added Flash programming support for Toshiba TMPM4G series devices.
  6. DLL: Added Flash programming support for Toshiba TMPM4K series devices.
  7. DLL: Added Flash programming support for iMXRT101x series devices.
  8. DLL: Added Info Flash Bank programming support for TI MSP432P401M and MSP432P401R devices.
  9. DLL: Added QSPI Flash programming support for Mediatek MT7686 series devices.
  10. DLL: Added Trusted Secure IP Authentication for Renesas RZ-A2M series devices.
  11. DLL: Added debug support for Syntacore SCR1 (RISC-V based). Fixed.
  12. DLL: Added flash programming support for Dialog Semiconductor DA1469x device family.
  13. DLL: Added flash programming support for NXP IMXRT1064 series devices.
  14. DLL: Added flash programming support for ST LPC54018JxM/LPC54S018JxM series devices.
  15. DLL: Added flash programming support for ST STM32L552xx and STM32L562xx series devices.
  16. DLL: Analog Devices nRF52811_xxAA: Added flash programming support.
  17. DLL: Dialog Semiconductor DA1469x: Under special circumstances, flash programming did not work. Fixed.
  18. DLL: Improved connect for MediaTek MT7686 series device.
  19. DLL: J-Link script files: When using the same label name in multiple functions, it could happen that a "goto" jumped to the wrong label. Fixed.
  20. DLL: Microchip IS208x: If user application enabled the WDT of the device, debugging did not work correctly (WDT kept running while core was halted). Fixed.
  21. DLL: NXP MK22FN512xxx12: Flash size assumed by the DLL was incorrect (256 KB instead of 512 KB). Fixed.
  22. DLL: NXP S32K14x (e.g. S32K144): Erasing more then one sector of the EEPROM did not work. Fixed.
  23. DLL: RISC-V: Enabled support for RTT and memory accesses while the CPU is running (requires RISC-V implementation with system bus access support)
  24. DLL: ST STM32F730xx / STM32F750xx: Added flash programming support (QSPI flash).
  25. DLL: ST STM32F730xx / STM32F750xx: Added flash programming support (internal flash).
  26. DLL: ST STM32H750xx: Added flash programming support (internal flash).
  27. DLL: ST STM32L010: Added flash programming support.
  28. DLL: Syntacore SCR1 (RISC-V based) device was not detected properly. Fixed.
  29. DLL: When connecting to a J-Link via TCP/IP and making use of auto-detect (not specifying an IP or S/N), the connection failed. Introduced with V6.42. Fixed.
  30. Firmware Flasher Portable PLUS: Update Batch file processing, now 16 setups supported
  31. Firmware Flasher: Added debug interface power down after stand-alone programming.
  32. Firmware Flasher: Added support for Cortex-M23/M33.
  33. Firmware Flasher: SPI interface supports up to 21MHz now. Idle state of SCK will no longer be forced to high-level.
  34. Firmware: J-Link EDU Mini: Enabled RTT support for RISC-V in firmware (requires RISC-V implementation with system bus access support)
  35. Firmware: J-Link EDU Mini: RISC-V: 8 and 16 bit write accesses to non-4-byte aligned addresses did not work correctly. Fixed.
  36. Firmware: J-Link EDU Mini: Syntacore SCR1 (RISC-V): Single stepping did not work reliably. Fixed.
  37. Firmware: J-Link EDU/BASE/PLUS V10: RISC-V: 8 and 16 bit write accesses to non-4-byte aligned addresses did not work correctly. Fixed.
  38. Firmware: J-Link EDU/BASE/PLUS V10: RISC-V: Enabled RTT support for RISC-V in firmware (requires RISC-V implementation with system bus access support)
  39. Firmware: J-Link EDU/BASE/PLUS V10: Syntacore SCR1 (RISC-V): Single stepping did not work reliably. Fixed.
  40. Firmware: J-Link OB-K22-SiFive: RISC-V: 8 and 16 bit write accesses to non-4-byte aligned addresses did not work correctly. Fixed.
  41. Firmware: J-Link PRO V4: Enabled RTT support for RISC-V in firmware (requires RISC-V implementation with system bus access support)
  42. Firmware: J-Link PRO V4: RISC-V: 8 and 16 bit write accesses to non-4-byte aligned addresses did not work correctly. Fixed.
  43. Firmware: J-Link PRO V4: Syntacore SCR1 (RISC-V): Single stepping did not work reliably. Fixed.
  44. Firmware: J-Link ULTRA+ V4: Enabled RTT support for RISC-V in firmware (requires RISC-V implementation with system bus access support)
  45. Firmware: J-Link ULTRA+ V4: RISC-V: 8 and 16 bit write accesses to non-4-byte aligned addresses did not work correctly. Fixed.
  46. Firmware: J-Link ULTRA+ V4: Syntacore SCR1 (RISC-V): Single stepping did not work reliably. Fixed.
  47. Firmware: J-Link-OB-XMC4200: Using the command in J-Link Commander before connecting to the target device could cause the J-Link firmware to hang and report a USB timeout. Fixed.
  48. J-Link STM32 Unlock utility: Added support to reset option bytes for STM32H7xxxx.
  49. RemoteServer: Added J-Link selection options.
  50. RemoteServer: Under special circumstances it could happen that in tunneled mode a connection to the tunnel server was closed immediately, even if the connection itself was fine. Fixed.
  51. Trace DLL: Added StartETB and StopETB JLinkScript file functions which can be used to replace the generic ETB init.

Version V6.42f (2019-02-26)

  1. DLL: Cypress PSoC4 family: Under special circumstnaces, connect did not work (e.g. on some CY8C4125xxx-Sxxx based device). Fixed.
  2. DLL: EFM32HG (4 KB variants; e.g. EFM32HG210F32): Flash programming did not work. Fixed.
  3. DLL: NXP LPC55xx / LPC55SXX: Under special circumstances, flash programming failed (verification error). Fixed.
  4. DLL: Renesas RX: Setting the authentication key via J-Link Command String (exec SetRXIDCode IDCode) did not work. Fixed.
  5. DLL: Under special circumstances, when a breakpoint was set on the upper and lower halfword of the same word, one of the two breakpoints could be ignored. Fixed.

Version V6.42e (2019-02-21)

  1. Commander: Commands "testnrspeed" and "testnwspeed" did not produce correct KB/s output. Fixed.
  2. DLL: A reset did not halt an Infineon XMC MCUs under special circumstances. Fixed.
  3. DLL: NXP S32k116: When programming the data flash @ 0x10000000, verifcation errors could occur. Fixed.
  4. DLL: RAM reinitialization during connect for NXP S32K1xx series devices, fixed.
  5. DLL: RISC-V: Improved log output for detected features of core.
  6. DLL: RISC-V: In case a RISC-V implementation only supported memory accesses via system bus but J-Link did not, no appropriate error message was output. Fixed.
  7. DLL: RISC-V: Under special circumstances, SiFive E31ARTY core (bitstream for ARTY board) was not recognized as a known core by J-Link. Fixed.
  8. DLL: RTT: Read speeds for RTT buffer sizes >2KB improved by 10-15%.
  9. DLL: ST STM32F7 QSPI: Increased the supported flash size up to 64 MB.
  10. Firmware Flasher: The PCode functions for "reset"/"after reset" were not always used. Fixed.
  11. Firmware: J-Link EDU Mini: RISC-V: Added support for memory accesses via system bus
  12. Firmware: J-Link EDU/BASE/PLUS V10: RISC-V: Added support for memory accesses via system bus
  13. Firmware: J-Link PRO V4: RISC-V: Added support for memory accesses via system bus
  14. Firmware: J-Link ULTRA+ V4: RISC-V: Added support for memory accesses via system bus
  15. J-Flash Lite: Support for debug interfaces other than JTAG broke. (Introduced in V6.42c) Fixed.
  16. Microchip (Atmel) SAM5x auxiliary space: Under special circumstances, flash programmign failed. Fixed.

Version V6.42d (2019-02-15)

  1. DLL: Improved ROM table scan for ARMv8-A based cores (e.g. Cortex-A53/72)
  2. DLL: Microchip IS208x: If FLASH_HDR_B1 was completely 0xFF (empty), it could happen that J-Link detected the wrong flash bank to be active. Fixed.
  3. DLL: Microchip IS208x: If control over target was lost, it could happen that the J-Link SW hung because of entering an endless loop. Fixed.
  4. DLL: Programming of Renesas RX230 / RX231 based devices could fail with programming errors when reprogramming flash at higher flash clocks (>= 36 MHz). Fixed.
  5. DLL: When connecting to an Renesas RX231 based device a warning did occur that an RX230 based device was configured. Fixed.
  6. DLL: When selecting generic Cortex-A53/72, the error message "Failed to power up DAP" could occur even if the DAP init was fine. Fixed.
  7. Firmware: J-Link-OB-K22-NordicSemi: VCOM: If Hardware flow control was used and the target interrupted the transmission by setting RTS == HIGH, it could happen that J-Link did not continue the transmission once RTS became LOW again. Fixed.
  8. J-Flash: Programming of Renesas RX230 / RX231 based devices could fail with programming errors when reprogramming flash at higher flash clocks (>= 36 MHz). Fixed.

Version V6.42c (2019-02-11)

  1. Commander: When having a comment '//' after the value/NumBytes on a w1/w2/w4 or mem command, it was accidentally interpreted as a memory zone. Fixed.
  2. DLL: Flash programming support for Dialog Semiconductor DA14195 series device, PLL settings were wrong. Fixed.
  3. DLL: When using streaming trace with timestamps, under very special circumstances a buffer overflow could happen. Fixed.
  4. GDBServer: cJTAG could not be selected in the TIF selection dialog. Fixed.
  5. J-Flash Lite: cJTAG could not be selected in the TIF selection dialog. Fixed.
  6. SDK: C sample projects for Visual Studio 2010 now statically link to MSVCRT.lib.
  7. SDK: VB6 sample project could not find JLinkARM.dll when debugging. Fixed.

Version V6.42b (2019-02-05)

  1. DLL: Connecting to J-Links via LAN-IP using identify by S/N did not work. Introduced in V6.42. Fixed.
  2. DLL: Connecting to SiFive RISC-V targets via cJTAG could fail if the device did not report a JTAG TAP Id. Fixed.
  3. DLL: Microchips SAMD51x: Flash programming performance improved.
  4. DLL: Microchips SAMD51x: Under special circumstances, user row programming did not work. Fixed.
  5. DLL: When selecting "E31ARTY" as device name, connecting via cJTAG failed. Fixed.
  6. Firmware: J-Link PRO V4: Added support for TIF Microchip 2-wire JTAG via TDI
  7. Firmware: J-Link ULTRA+ V4: Added support for TIF Microchip 2-wire JTAG via TDI
  8. GDBServer: Cortex-M: Reading/Writing of single precision FPU registers s23-s31 did not work. Fixed.
  9. GDBServer: Cortex-M: Writing of double precision FPU registers d0-d15 did not work. Fixed.
  10. GDBServer: When register index list contained gaps, it was possible that writing a single register after the first gap resulted in an incorrect register being written. Fixed.

Version V6.42a (2019-02-01)

  1. DLL: SPIFI flash programming speed improved by 10 to 15% for certain devices. Affected device series: Microchip SAMV7, Broadcom BCM89107, Marvell MW30x, Maxim MAX3265, NXP LPC18xx, NXP LPC43xx, NXP LPC408x, NXP LPC54xx, Renesas RZ/A1L, Renesas RZ/A1H, Renesas RZ/T1, Renesas Synergy, Xilinx Zynq7000.
  2. DLL: Sector size of NXP MKV42Fxxx, MKV44Fxxx and MKV46Fxxx devices was incorrect. Fixed.
  3. DLL: improved connect sequence for TI AM335x series devices.
  4. J-Flash: Added support to write to the DEV_RAM on the TI PGA900, if memory remapping is set.

Version V6.42 (2019-01-30)

  1. DLL: Adapted SPIFI FLASH programming algorithms according to improved SPIFI lib.
  2. DLL: Added ETB trace support for Renesas RZ/T1 M3 subcore.
  3. DLL: Added Flash programming support for LPC55xx series devices.
  4. DLL: Added Flash programming support for Analog ADuCM355 series devices.
  5. DLL: Added Flash programming support for Cypress CY8C6xxA series devices.
  6. DLL: Added Flash programming support for Maxim MAX32665, MAX32666, MAX32667 and MAX32668 series devices.
  7. DLL: Added Flash programming support for Microchip ATSAMR34 and ATSAMR35 series devices.
  8. DLL: Added Flash programming support for Nuvoton NuMicro M2351xxxx series devices.
  9. DLL: Added Flash programming support for ST STM32G0 series devices.
  10. DLL: Added HYPERFLASH programming support for Renesas RZ/A2M series devices.
  11. DLL: Added HYPERFLASH programming support via QSPI for Renesas RZ/A2M series devices.
  12. DLL: Added OCTA FLASH programming support for Renesas RZ/A2M series devices.
  13. DLL: Added QSPI FLASH programming support for Renesas RZ/A2M series devices.
  14. DLL: Added QSPI Flash programming support for Dialog Semiconductor DA14x95 series devices.
  15. DLL: Added QSPI-Flash programming support for CYW43907 series devices.
  16. DLL: Added bootloader FLASH section for EFR32 series devices.
  17. DLL: Added command string "ResetJLink" to reset a J-Link (Currently only available for JLink-OB-SAM3U128-NordicSemi)
  18. DLL: Added command string "SetcJTAGInitMode"
  19. DLL: Added debug support for Renesas RZ/T1 M3 subcore.
  20. DLL: Added debug support for TI AM437X series devices.
  21. DLL: Added option byte programming for MindMotion MM32xxx series devices.
  22. DLL: Added read protection and unprotect mechanism for MindMotion MM32xxx series devices.
  23. DLL: Added support for SiFive RISC-V based targets via cJTAG
  24. DLL: Added support for TI PGA900
  25. DLL: Added support for command string "InvalidateCPUState"
  26. DLL: Added support for command string "RestoreDownloadAfterReset"
  27. DLL: Added support for some new Cypress PSoC4 devices.
  28. DLL: Extended support for PW-protected tunnel connections as well as connections to custom tunnel servers
  29. DLL: Implemented QSPI flash programming support for SiFive FE310
  30. DLL: Implemented support for tunnel connections via custom tunnel server and port
  31. DLL: Implemented support for tunnel connections via nickname
  32. DLL: J-Link script files: Added constant JLINK_TIF_MC2WJTAG_TDI
  33. DLL: J-Link script files: Added pseudo variable JLINK_FLASH_DownloadAddr
  34. DLL: J-Link script files: Added pseudo variable JLINK_FLASH_NumBytesDownloaded
  35. DLL: J-Link script files: Added support for API calls SPI2FE_ReadBits() and SPI2FE_WriteBits()
  36. DLL: J-Link script files: Added support for BeforeResetTarget() function
  37. DLL: J-Link script files: Added support for sizeof() operator
  38. DLL: J-Link script files: Comparisons with more than 2 operands did not work properly. Example: if (Addr || Addr1 || Addr2) { ... }. Fixed.
  39. DLL: Memory overlap issue for NXP MKxx series devices, fixed.
  40. DLL: New ST STM32L4xx devices show different IDCODE needed for Flash protection handling. Added IDCODE for L45x and L46x series.
  41. DLL: On some cores which require certain registers to be restored in HW by J-Link on each Go() / Step(), it could happen that some of these registers were not restored correctly. Fixed.
  42. DLL: Renesas RX66T group devices: Added data flash programming support
  43. DLL: Renesas RX66T group devices: Added debugging support for: R5F566TA, R5F566TE, R5F566TF, R5F566TK
  44. DLL: Renesas RX66T group devices: Added program flash programming support
  45. DLL: SiFive FE310: Reduced time needed for reset from app. 3 seconds to slightly above 1 second (cannot be reduced further because core does not become responsive before that)
  46. DLL: Size of RAM for NXP MK22FX512xxx series devices to 128kB, corrected.
  47. DLL: Some NXP LPC802 / LPC804 passed by IAR EWARM where not accepted by the J-Link DLL. Fixed.
  48. DLL: The RAM size of NXP LPC804 devices was incorrect (2 KB instead of 4 KB). Fixed.
  49. DLL: Updated flash programming support for Cypress CY8C6xx6 and CY8C6xx7 series devices.
  50. DLL: Warning "Mis-aligned memory write: ..." printed garbage for
    and . Fixed.
  51. Firmware: Flasher PORTABLE PLUS: Added stand-alone programming for RX63 MCUs.
  52. Firmware: Flasher PORTABLE PLUS: Added universal flash loader support for PIC16 derivatives
  53. Firmware: Flasher PRO V4: Added stand-alone programming for RX63 MCUs.
  54. Firmware: Flasher PRO V4: Added universal flash loader support for PIC16 derivatives
  55. Firmware: J-Link EDU Mini: RISC-V: Added support for cJTAG
  56. Firmware: J-Link EDU Mini: RISC-V: Improved timeout handling in case BUSY responses were sent by the debug module interface.
  57. Firmware: J-Link EDU/BASE/PLUS V10: Added support for target interface "Microchip 2-wire JTAG via TDI"
  58. Firmware: J-Link EDU/BASE/PLUS V10: RISC-V: Added support for cJTAG
  59. Firmware: J-Link EDU/BASE/PLUS V10: RISC-V: Improved timeout handling in case BUSY responses were sent by the debug module interface.
  60. Firmware: J-Link OB-K22-SiFive: Drag & Drop: Improved error message of FAIL.txt in case a datafile contained addresses that are not in the target's flash range.

  10. J-Link Commander: Commands "testwspeed" and "testrspeed" did not show speed correctly (Introduced in V6.34). Fixed.

  1. DLL: J-Link Lite FSL: When having multiple of these J-Links connected, connection dialogs have shown the same S/N (2147483647) for all of them. Fixed.

    static const char* xxx= ;

  7. J-Flash: J-Flash did not return in error in case of flash information could not be determined. Fixed.
  8. DLL: Unsecuring a TI CC25xx or CC26xx device could fail. Fixed.

  10. DLL: Under certain circumstances MTB addresses set by user were reset for Cortex-M33 target devices. Fixed.

  12. DLL: OpenSDA running J-Link firmware could not be used with NXP devices like i.MXRT1052 (J-Link software complained about silicon vendor limit of OpenSDA). Fixed.
  13. DLL: Under special circumstances, memory zones for Cortex-A/R devices were not shown correctly in Ozone. Fixed.
  14. J-Link Commander: Improved output of memory zones
  15. RTT Viewer: If sending input fails, application could get stuck in a loop. Fixed.
  16. DLL: Cortex-M23/M33: Detection of CoreSight components did not work properly (e.g. different components were identified as identical ones by mistake). Fixed.
  17. UM08001: Added description of J-Flash Lite to manual
  18. Firmware: VCOM: It could happen that on a COM port open the J-Link internal "hardware flow control in use" detection was not reset properly. Fixed.
    Affected firmwares: JLink-OB-SAM3U128-NordicSemi
  19. Firmware: When selecting specific interface speeds and the initial connect via SWD interface failed,
    it could happen that the J-Link firmware hang and USB timeouts occurred when the DLL tried the fallback connect method. Fixed.

  22. DLL: For current J-Trace PRO revisions which support streaming trace via USB3, it could happen that the warning "For max. trace throughput, please connect J-Trace via IP" appeared. Fixed.

  56. DLL: Writing to memory via zones could write wrong data. Fixed.
  57. DLL: Calls to JLINK_STRACE_GetInstStats() were not thread safe (other API functions could be called in parallel, messing up DLL internal status data). Fixed.
  58. J-Flash Lite: File dialog did not allow selecting network resources. Fixed.
  59. Software package (Windows): In Windows 10 and later, when having multiple versions of the J-Link software installed, they were presented in a messy way in the start menu. Fixed.
  60. DLL: Added Scriptfile function SWO_EnableTarget() for non generic SWO configurations.
  61. DLL: Renamed Scriptfile function GetSWOBaseClock() to SWO_GetSWOBaseClock().
  62. J-FLASH SPI CL: Added CL option -jflashlog and -jlinklog.
  63. J-FLASH SPI CL: Streamlined CL options to follow descriptions in user manual.
  64. DLL: Added flash programming support for NXP Kinetis K27FA (MK27FN2M0Axxx15) and K28FA (MK28FN2M0Axxx15).
  65. DLL: Added flash programming support for TI CC3220xx devices
  66. DLL: Added programming support for ST STM32F2xxx Option Bytes.
  67. DLL: Added programming support for internal flash of GigaDevice GD32F1xx, GD32F2xx, GD32F3xx and GD32F4xx series.
  68. DLL: NXP iMX7D: Added QSPI flash programming support.
  69. DLL: Open flash loader did not work correctly (DLL could complain about not finding some symbols in the ELF file). Introduced with V6.30i (release) and V6.31f (beta). Fixed.
  70. DLL: Silicon Labs EFM32GG11Bxx devices and bootloader flash added, also for EFM32TG11BxxxF64 and EFM32TG11BxxxF128
  71. J-Flash: NXP iMXRT102x: Added QSPI-Flash programming support.
  72. DLL: Added support for RISC-V with V0.11 (legacy) debug interface.
  73. J-Flash SPI: Some SPI flashes listed as supported were not detected properly. Fixed.
  74. Affected flashes: ISSI IS25LQ080B
    ISSI IS25LQ016B
    ISSI IS25LQ032B
  75. Firmware: Configuring fixed VTref of <= 1.2V was not catched and ignored properly. Fixed.
    Affected firmwares: J-Link BASE V10

Version V6.30k (2018-04-09)

  1. DLL: If both, a JLinkDevices.xml and JLinkDevices.ref was present in the DLL dir, the XML always had priority which made it impossible to update SEGGER Embedded Studio installations via new J-Link software packages. Fixed.
  2. DLL: Open flash loader did not work correctly (DLL could complain about not finding some symbols in the ELF file). Introduced with V6.30i (release) and V6.31f (beta). Fixed.
  3. DLL: Some old SiLabs J-Link OBs are running a buggy firmware that did not work well with current J-Link software versions. Fixed.
  4. J-Flash SPI CL: Possible vulnerability in -open command line option when passing formatter strings like xxx%p%p%p. Fixed.
  5. J-Flash: *.s37 could not be selected in the data file dialog. Fixed.
  6. J-Flash: When creating a new project for a Renesas RX device and then open a data file, followed by a "Save Flasher data file" select, it could happen that the Flasher data file was empty (header data only, no payload data). Fixed.
  7. J-Link Commander: Commander could crash on command file execution if a line in the command file contained more than 511 characters. Fixed.
  8. J-Link Configurator: A crash could happen when hitting "Update firmware of selected emulators" but not having any emulators selected. Fixed.

  8. J-Link Commander: Exec command verifybin did not handle correctly on failed verify. Fixed.
  9. Firmware: When selecting an interface != JTAG, it could happen that a glitch was output on the TCK and/or TMS pin of J-Link (this caused problems when performing the ASC -> SWD BMI switching sequence for Infineon XMC1xxx series devices). Fixed.

  7. J-Flash: The power options were not handled correctly. Fixed.
  8. J-Flash: Under special circumstances, when changing the MCU device in the project settings, it could happen that an additional "Auto detection" flash bank has been added. Fixed.
  9. J-Flash: When connecting to the J-Link for downloading config files, the connect was rejected, if a fixed VTref setting was applied. Fixed.
  10. Flasher firmware: The flasher did not accept a new command in case of an "#auto patch" command failed due to invalid parameters. Fixed.
  11. Flasher firmware: The flasher did not power down the target, if the VTRef monitor reported an error. Fixed.

Version V6.30g (2018-03-12)

  1. DLL (Linux/macOS): If JLINKARM_Open() failed and no JLINKARM_Close() was called afterwards (which is allowed due to the API spec.) it could happen that the process crashed on unload of J-Link DLL (Mainly happened in SEGGER Embedded Studio). Fixed.
  2. DLL: Connecting to fab. new Analog Devices CM40x revision 2 or later series devices could fail. Fixed.
  3. DLL: J-Link OB on Holt IC boards with S/N 302113761 - 302113860 incorrectly reported "Renesas" as silicon vendor limit. Fixed.
  4. DLL: JLINK_FUNC_CAN_ACC_MEM_WHILE_RUNNING did not distinguish between 1 and 2 which allows detection of background access support and stop mode access support. Fixed.
  5. DLL: Reverted change (V6.30f) in Flash loader for STM32F401CC devices. More information how to program STEVAL-FCU001V1 can be found in SEGGER Wiki.
  6. DLL: SiLabs EFM32/EFR32/EZR32: Support for voltage scaling mode broke support for some EFM32 series devices (e.g. EFM32WG series). Introduced in V6.30e. Fixed.
  7. DLL: TI RM47L series devices could halt on SVC exceptions even if user did not set vector catch in IDE. Fixed.
  8. DLL: TI RM4xL series devices could halt on SVC exceptions even if user did not set vector catch in IDE. Fixed.
  9. DLL: TI TMS570 series devices could halt on SVC exceptions even if user did not set vector catch in IDE. Fixed.
  10. DLL: Under special circumstances, flash programming on Cypress S6J32x /S6J33x (Traveo) series devices could fail. Fixed.
  11. DLL: When using an old J-Link with Keil MDK-ARM and Cortex-R4 based devices, the error message "The connected J-Link does not support the requested memory access (Flags = 02000000)". Fixed.
  12. Package (Windows): Added version number to shortcuts in start menu to be able to distinguish between multiple versions in Windows 10 start menu and Windows 7 start menu search
  13. Flasher firmware: A communication timeout could occur while creating the secure area or deleting files. Fixed.

Version V6.22e (2018-01-08)

  1. DLL: Connecting to NXP i.MX6UL and i.MX6ULL series devices failed. Introduced with V6.22. Fixed.
  2. DLL: Internal flash programming support for NXP LPC8N04 device added.
  3. DLL: Message box "Found active soft BPs when downloading to flash" could appear. Fixed.
  4. DLL: NXP S32K142: The device was configured as Cortex-M0 but it is a Cortex-M4. Fixed.
  5. Flasher: Under special circumstances e.g. in case of the device is in some kind of low power mode, flash programming in stand-alone mode failed (e.g. EM357 devices). Fixed.
  6. J-Flash SPI: Erase timed out for SPI flashes with a busy bit (e.g. Adesto AT25SF64). Fixed.
  7. J-Flash: If a flash algorithm specified page sizes > 2KB, generation of FLASHER.DAT, for stand-alone mode operation, failed. Fixed.
  8. J-Link SDK: Added new indirect API function "JLINK_IFUNC_SCRIPTFILE_EXEC" which can be used to execute a specific function from the actual selected J-Link script file.

Version V6.22d (2017-12-14)

  1. DLL / Flasher stand-alone mode: There has been a regression regarding the flash programming speed of Marvell 88MW300 series devices. Introduced in V6.16i. Fixed.
  2. DLL: Fixed programming speed regression for CFI based flash algorithms (AMD). Introduced in V6.xx. Fixed.
  3. DLL: Flash programming of the Flex NVM area of NXP MWCT101xS series devices did not work. Fixed.
  4. DLL: TI CC2538: Unlocking of secured devices did not work. Fixed.
  5. DLL: The sector size of NXP S32K142 series devices was incorrect (4KB instead of 2KB). This could cause issues during flash programming. Fixed.
  6. DLL: Updated the flashloader for Analog Devices ADUCM4x50 (erase timing updated).
  7. J-Flash: Added a new tab (Performance), which can be used to configure certain optimizations which are valid for all actions in J-Flash (Production Programming & Manual Programming).
  8. J-Flash: J-Flash does no longer perform a erase prior "Manual Programming" -> "Program" or "Manual Programming" -> "Program & Verify".

Version V6.22c (2017-12-08)

  1. DLL (SDK): Added JLINK_DEVICE_GetIndex() to J-Link API.
  2. DLL (SDK): Added JLINK_DEVICE_SelectDialog() to J-Link API.
  3. DLL (Windows): If FlashBPs needed to be removed on DLL close, GUI thread was not exited properly which could cause J-Link tray icon to stay in task bar until the whole process was exited. Fixed.
  4. DLL: Added flash programming support for Maxim MAX32558 series devices.
  5. DLL: NXP LPC540xx: Under special circumstances, flash programming (QSPI) did not work. Fixed.
  6. DLL: Under certain circumstances ETM Trace with 3rd party debug software was not working correctly, introduced with V6.20g. Fixed.
  7. DLL: When having multiple connections to a J-Link open, no error was indicated if J-Link firmware could not allocate connection context. Fixed.
  8. Firmware: J-Link OB-MB9AF312K-Spansion did not allow debugging of Cypress devices that were originally Spansion devices. Fixed.
  9. Firmware: Under special circumstances, connecting to XMC1000 series devices did not work. Fixed.
  10. Flasher Portable PLUS: Firmware update failed. Introduced in V6.22. Fixed.
  11. J-Flash SPI CL: Under special circumstances, the command line version did not return an value != 0 in case of error. Fixed.
  12. J-Link Commander: MacAddr command: Wrong MACAddr was shown for unknown J-Link models. Fixed.
  13. Firmware: When having multiple connections to a J-Link open, J-Link firmware could crash if it not allocate connection context. Fixed.
  14. Firmware: RTT did not work correctly on big endian targets. Fixed.
    Affected firmwares: J-Link BASE V10
    J-Link PLUS V10
    J-Link EDU V10
    J-Link BASE V9
    J-Link PLUS V9
    J-Link EDU V9

    J-Trace PRO V2 Cortex-M
    J-Trace PRO V2 Cortex

    J-Link Lite Cortex-M V9
    J-Link EDU Mini

Version V6.22b (2017-12-06)

  1. DLL: Opening multiple connections to a J-Link could fail on some current models. Introduced with V6.22a Windows Hibernate workaround. Fixed.

Version V6.22a (2017-11-28)

  1. DLL: Added CORESIGHT_SetCSTFBaseAddr exec command to be able to set trace funnel base address over scriptfile should automatic detection through ROM table not be available.
  2. DLL: Added NVM user row programming support for SAM4L series devices.
  3. DLL: Atmel SAMD20: Under special circumstances, the user row could not be programmed. Fixed.
  4. DLL: Connect sequence of Infineon XMC4000 series devices could not be overwritten via J-Link script files. Fixed.
  5. DLL: For some devices (e.g. Synergy S7G2) Coresight addresses were set incorrectly. Introduced with V6.20g. Fixed.
  6. DLL: NXP LPC1850: QSPI flash programming did not work when using a S25FL129P as target SPI flash. Fixed.
  7. DLL: Reset sequence of Infineon XMC4000 series devices could not be overwritten via J-Link script files. Fixed.
  8. DLL: S32K144: Unlocking procedure was not reliable. Fixed.
  9. DLL: Some Infineon XMC100 device names (e.g. xmc1100) were not accepted by the J-Link DLL. Fixed.
  10. DLL: Some J-Link OBs on eval boards from Engenuics (e.g. Razor Board 2) could only be used with the NordicSemi nRF device on the board but not with the Microchip SAM3U. Introduced in V6.22. Fixed.
  11. DLL: Some batches of J-Link EDU Mini did not report to have a valid FlashBP license. Fixed.
  12. DLL: When exiting Hibernate mode under Windows 7 / Windows 10 it could happen that J-Link became unresponsive to certain commands. Fixed.
  13. DLL: If one instance had a connection to a new USB 3.0 based J-Trace model open, this J-Trace was not listed in Configurator anymore. Fixed.
    Affected J-Trace models: J-Trace PRO V2 Cortex-M
    J-Trace PRO V2 Cortex
  14. J-Link Commander: Added command "VTREF" to set a fixed VTref for J-Links that support it
  15. J-Link SWOViewer: Added SWOClock Combobox and renamed TRACECLK Combobox to CPUClock. Now the user has the option to select the SWOClock speed manually. Default is maximum supported SWOSpeed by target device.
    Affected firmwares: J-Link BASE V10

    J-Link Lite Cortex-M V9

  16. Firmware: Added support for setting fixed VTref.

Version V6.22 (2017-11-24)

  1. DLL (Linux): Under very special circumstances a deadlock could occur due to incorrect handling of WaitForMutexTimed()
  2. DLL (SDK): JLINKARM_ReadRegs(): If one or more registers in the list could not be read, the following valid ones were placed at the wrong position in the output buffer. Fixed.
  3. DLL: Added QSPI flash programming support for NXP LPC540xx series devices.
  4. DLL: Added command string SetDisableSkipBlankDataOnProg. Forces J-Link/Flasher to also program all areas in the data file that are filled with the erased value (usually 0xFF)
  5. DLL: Added flash programming support for Cypress PSoC 4100 Plus series devices.
  6. DLL: Added flash programming support for Cypress PSoC 4100S series devices.
  7. DLL: Added flash programming support for Cypress S6J3300 series devices.
  8. DLL: Added flash programming support for Maxim MAX32510 series devices.
  9. DLL: Added flash programming support for Maxim MAX32600 series devices.
  10. DLL: Added flash programming support for Maxim MAX32650.
  11. DLL: Added flash programming support for NXP LPC802 series devices.
  12. DLL: Added flash programming support for NXP S32K116 and S32K118 series devices.
  13. DLL: Added flash programming support for Qorvo UE878 series devices.
  14. DLL: Added flash programming support for ST BlueNRG2 series devices.
  15. DLL: Added flash programming support for ST STM32L4R and STM32L4S series devices.
  16. DLL: Added flash programming support for TI MSP432E series devices.
  17. DLL: Added native pin trace support for STM32L4R/S device family based on STM32L4R9I - EVAL board.
  18. DLL: Added user row programming support for Atmel (Microchip) SAMC20, SAMC21, SAMDA and SAML22 series devices.
  19. DLL: Added write protected device detection for Nuvoton NUC1xx, NUC4xx and M45x series devices.
  20. DLL: For some very old J-Link OBs mounted on IAR MB9BG618T-SK boards, the error message that the OB has been designed to work with devices from "Renesas only" popped up. Fixed.
  21. DLL: For some very old J-Link OBs mounted on IAR TMPM369-SK boards, the error message that the OB has been designed to work with devices from "Renesas only" popped up. Fixed.
  22. DLL: Implemented graphs for target power consumption, target voltage, ... in web based control panel.
  23. DLL: Implemented support for script file function to retrieve SWO base clock for devices where SWO base clock is not CPU clock (e.g. SiLabs EFM32 and NordicSemi nRF52)
  24. DLL: J-Link Lite-ADI (Analog Devices) probes could not be used with ADuCM450. Fixed.
  25. DLL: NXP K32W_M4: Changed reset behavior of the M4 to perform a ordinary reset (reset via system reset request).
  26. DLL: NXP S32K148: The flash size specified in the J-Link software was incorrect (2 MB instead of 1.5MB). Fixed.
  27. DLL: Open Flashloader: The Open Flashloader now allows to specify less than 512 elements in the SECTOR_INFO struct which is part of the "FlashDevice".
  28. DLL: QSPI flash programming did not work for empty NXP LPC540xx and LPC54S0xx series devices. Fixed.
  29. DLL: RISC-V: Flash breakpoints did work properly if interrupts were active/enabled
  30. DLL: Renesas Synergy S5D9: Added flash programming support for the configuration flash area.
  31. DLL: ST STM32F7: Added support to program the internal flash trough the ITCM memory space.
  32. DLL: Some J-Link OBs on eval boards from Engenuics (e.g. Razor Board 2) threw the error message "This J-Link has been designed to work with devices made by Atmel only", while there is a Nordic Semi device on the board. Fixed.
  33. DLL: When debugging on RISC-V based devices, a reset sometimes did not halt the MCU before it executed some user code. Fixed.
  34. DLLUpdater: SEGGER Embedded Studio RISC-V was not offered for DLL updates. Fixed.
  35. J-Flash SPI: "-speed" command line option was not evaluated. Fixed.
  36. J-Flash SPI: Added new example project which performs a protection unlock on connect for Adesto AT25DF081 SPI flashes.
  37. J-Flash: Added new command line argument "-setcpuidcode".
  38. J-Link Commander: Added new command "ExpDevListXML" which can be used to export the entire device list + aliases in a xml formatted file.
  39. RTT tab in web based control panel did not lock correctly when adding RTT printf data. Fixed.
  40. Trace: Updated script file for Atmel SAMA5D2x devices to support ETB trace.
  41. Firmware: Under very special circumstances, download into RAM on Renesas RZ/A1H devices was factor 3 slower when running a firmware from the V6.20 J-Linmk software series. Fixed.
    Affected firmwares: J-Link BASE V10
    J-Link PLUS V10

Version V6.20i (2017-11-17)

  1. DLL (SDK): Added new index for JLINKARM_GetDebugInfo(). JLINKARM_DEBUG_INFO_HAS_FPU_INDEX
  2. DLL (SDK): J-Link shared lib did not work on older Linux systems that only provide libudev.so.0.x (dependency on libudev.so.1 present). Fixed.
  3. DLL (SDK): JLink_x64.lib had dependencies on _GSHandlerCheck() and __security_check_coockie() which caused problems when using this lib with MinGW. Fixed.
  4. DLL: Added SiFive E31ARTY as supported device name.
  5. DLL: Analog Devices ADuCM405x: Updated the flash algorithm with a new version which sets the ECC bits.
  6. DLL: Flash programming of Cypress PSoC6 series did not work. Fixed.
  7. DLL: JTAG Id of NXP iMX8 DAP was not recognized. Fixed. (A53 / A72 cores are not supported yet!)
  8. DLL: NXP: Updated the alias device table as some devices were not recognized.
  9. DLL: Silicon Labs EFM32JG12BxxxF1024 was not recognized by the J-Link DLL. Fixed.
  10. DLL: Atmel SAMV7: From now, we support flash programming through the mirror address at 0x00000000.
  11. DLL: Some Realtek devices were identified incorrectly, causing memory accesses that crossed a 1 KB boundary, to not work correctly. Fixed.
  12. J-Link Commander: FPU registers were not shown for Cortex-M23 / M33 based devices. Fixed.
  13. J-Link Commander: J-Trace Pro MACAddress was not printed in Commander correctly when requested. Fixed.
  14. Open Flashloader: Default programing timeout changed to 1 second. Should a flashloader be used with a lower value it will be overwritten to 1 second.
  15. Open Flashloader: SPI Flashloader on NXP iMX7ULP series devices could timeout under certain circumstances. Fixed.

Version V6.20h (2017-10-27)

  1. DLL: Cypress CY8C4126xxx-Sxxx_ID25x / CY8C4146xxx-Sxxx_ID25x: Page size of the internal flash, used during programming procedure, was incorrect. Fixed.
  2. DLL: Flasher V3 was not able to detect a STM32L4 series device. Fixed.
  3. DLL: When using an old Flasher V3 with a target device which requires special handling on connect, a communication time out occurred. Fixed.
  4. J-Flash SPI: J-Flash SPI did not evaluate the "Disconnect after each operation" setting. Fixed.

Version V6.20g (2017-10-20)

  1. DLL: Added ETM backtrace support via J-Trace for Cortex-A9 + PTM (e.g. Renesas RZ/A1H)
  2. DLL: Added Trace Pin initialization for Renesas RZ/A1H to generic part.
  3. DLL: Added command string "CORESIGHT_SetMTBBufBaseAddr"
  4. DLL: Added command string "CORESIGHT_SetTFEnableMask"
  5. DLL: Added flash programming support for TI MSP432E series devices.
  6. DLL: Cortex-M23/M33: ROM table detection did not detect ITM component properly. Fixed.
  7. DLL: Cortex-M23: ROM table detection did not detect MTB-M23 component properly. Fixed.
  8. DLL: Improved single stepping speed in case trace is active
  9. DLL: Infineon TLE985x: Verify of the NACNAD area failed erroneously. Fixed.
  10. DLL: NXP Kinetis KL46 series: MTB tracing did not work properly. Fixed.
  11. DLL: Open Flashloader: Download failed on Cortex-A/R device. Introduced with 6.20b. Fixed.
  12. DLL: Windows 64-bit: Message box "The connected J-Link has been designed to work with devices made by xxx..." could crash debug session. Fixed.
  13. J-Flash: No target interface was suggested for devices with Cortex-M3 r2p1 core. Fixed.
  14. J-Flash: No target interface was suggested for devices with RX65N/RX24T/RX130 core. Fixed.
  15. J-Flash: Secure Target could fail if exit steps were specified. Fixed.
  16. J-Link CCS: From now, a J-Link script file can be specified in the target configuration dialog.
  17. J-Link Commander: No target interface was suggested for devices with Cortex-M3 r2p1 core. Fixed.
  18. J-Link Commander: No target interface was suggested for devices with RX65N/RX24T/RX130 core. Fixed.
  19. RTTViewer: RTTViewer now uses the standard device selection dialog.

Version V6.20f (2017-10-13)

  1. DLL (Linux): When using streaming trace, the error "unknown trace packet found" could occur, even if everything was fine. Fixed.
  2. DLL (SDK): C# sample could crash in case a unknown or no device was selected. Fixed.
  3. DLL/J-Flash: UNC network shares were accidentally handled as relative paths. Fixed.
  4. DLL: Added flash programming support for NXP LPC802 series devices.
  5. DLL: Added new command string (SetHostIF ) which allows to configure the host interface (e.g. IP=192.168.0.12).
  6. DLL: Added support for multiple instances of the J-Link web control panel (e.g. in multiple Embedded Studio sessions etc.)
  7. DLL: Flash programming for TI TMS570 did not work correctly. Introduced in V6.20b. Fixed.
  8. DLL: Infineon TLE985x: Connect did not work and under special circumstances, flash programming failed. Fixed.
  9. DLL: ON Semiconductor RSL10: RTT did not work due to incorrect work RAM was used. Fixed.
  10. DLL: ON Semiconductor RSL10: System clock was restored incorrectly. Fixed.
  11. DLL: Open Flashloader: When issuing two erase operations in a row, the Init() and UnInit() functions have been called in an incorrect order. Fixed.
  12. DLL: ST STM32F0: Attach did not work. Fixed.
  13. GDBServer: A buffer overflow could occur, if a symbol name in the RTOS plugin was longer than 31 characters. Fixed.
  14. J-Flash: J-Flash ignored invalid command line options. From now, J-Flash handles invalid / unknown command line options as error.

Version V6.20e (2017-10-06)

  1. DLL: Flash programming of Infineon TLE98xx series devices did not work. Fixed.
  2. DLL: Silicon Labs EFM32TG: Connecting to a secured device failed. Fixed.
  3. DLL: Under certain circumstances, connecting to NXP Kinetis V5x devices did not work. Fixed.
  4. Flasher Firmware: Stand-alone mode programming failed when using SPC560D30/SPC560D40 target devices. Fixed.
  5. J-Flash SPI: Flash programming did not work for Micron SPI flashes >= 16 MB. Fixed.
  6. J-Link PRO Webserver: Target power consumption is displayed in uA, but unit was displayed as "mA". Fixed.

Version V6.20d (2017-09-29)

  1. DLL/J-Flash: Data flash could not be programmed on SPC560D30/SPC560D40 devices. Fixed.
  2. DLL: Added new aliases for new and existing NXP Kinetis & LPC series devices, as some IDEs were using names that caused an "unknown device" error message with J-Link. Fixed.
  3. DLL: Improved Atmel SAMD20 flash download speed.
  4. DLL: Open Flashloader: The incorrect sector information (the one from the JLinkDevices.XLM) have been showed in the device selection dialog. Fixed.
  5. Flasher: Flash programming of Atmel SAMD20 series devices did not work in stand-alone mode. Fixed.
  6. Flasher: Under special circumstances (device empty), flash programming of NXP SKEAZNxx and KE0x series devices failed. Fixed.
  7. J-Flash: Added example project for SiliconLabs EF32G1 series, which enables the security as part of the exit steps. (EFR32BG1BxxxF256_EnableSecurity.jflash)
  8. J-Flash: In command line mode, saving a flasher data file did not work. Fixed.
  9. J-Flash: In command line mode, some error messages were not logged. Fixed.
  10. J-Flash: Under special circumstances (device empty), flash programming of NXP SKEAZNxx and KE0x series devices failed. Fixed.
  11. J-Link Commander: J-Link Commander did not quit if exitonerror was active and the "connect" command failed. Fixed.
  12. J-Link TI CCS plugin: Under certain conditions, e.g. using an AM335x device, starting a debug session did not work. Fixed.
  13. RTTViewer: Terminals were cleared on disconnect for no reason. Fixed.

Version V6.20c (2017-09-26)

  1. Firmware: RISC-V: Under special circumstances, flash programming could fail when checking IsHalted() state of CPU, before starting flash programming. Fixed.

  1. DLL: ST STM32F4: Sector erased failed on dual bank flash devices (2 MB). Fixed.
  2. DLL: CMSIS / Open Flashloader: From now, we use the "TimeoutErase" for chip erase instead of the fixed timeout of 20 seconds.

  4. J-Flash: When specifying a data file relative to the project file, the data file could not be opened. Fixed.
  5. DLL: When erasing sector 0 of Cypress S6E1C series devices, the trimming data were erased, too. Fixed.

Version V6.18b (2017-08-18)

  1. DLL: NXP K32W Series: Added flash programming + full debug support for the Cortex-M0 core.
  2. DLL: Added flash programming support for ONSemi RSL10 series devices.
  3. DLL: RTT did not work correctly on Cortex-A and Cortex-R based devices. Introduced in V6.16. Fixed.

Version V6.18a (2017-08-11)

  1. DLL: Added flash programming support for Microsemi M2S060 series devices.
  2. DLL: Added flash programming support for Nordic Semiconductor nRF52810_xxAA series devices.
  3. DLL: Added support for Renesas RX65N series.
  4. DLL: CMSIS / Open Flashloader: The DLL crashed when using large flash algorithms ( > 64 KB ). Fixed.
  5. DLL: CMSIS / Open Flashloader: The J-Link DLL was not able to handle algorithms with a RAM usage (RAMCode size + Page Size == data block size) > 32 KB. Fixed.
  6. DLL: Cortex-M23 / M33 core was no longer found on some buggy FPGA setups which provide incorrect ROM table information. Introduced with V6.18. Fixed.

  10. STM32 Unlock: Factory default value for FLASH_OPTCR1 of STM32F7xx series devices was incorrect. Fixed.

Version V6.16i (2017-07-21)

  1. DLL: Added support for GigaDevice (Q)SPI NOR flashes:

  4. DLL: CMSIS / Open Flashloader: From now, we use the timeouts specified in the "FlashDevice" structure for program ("TimeoutProg") and erase sector ("TimeoutErase").

  7. DLL: Marvell 88MW300: Improved verification speed for QSPI programming (Example: 1 MB took ~8 seconds, now: ~3 seconds)
  8. DLL: QSPI flash programming did not work with Cypress S25FL064L SPI flashes (e.g. on the LPC4330). Fixed.
  9. GDBServer: Command line version now outputs full, passed command line via stdout.
  10. GDBServer: Server could hang and did not respond to any pause/exit etc. requests anymore if target application used semihosting with a getchar() putchar() echo implementation. Fixed.
  11. J-Flash SPI: Added example project for Cypress FM25CL64B SPI / F-RAM flash (Cypress_FM25CL64B.jflash).
  12. J-Flash SPI: Added support for Cypress S25FL064L SPI flash.
  13. J-Flash: Buttons in general options dialog overlapped with controls. Fixed.
  14. J-Flash: CMSIS / Open Flashloader: Added support for check blank via read back.
  15. J-Flash: CMSIS / Open Flashloader: If programming failed in J-Flash, an incorrect address has been reported in the error message. Fixed.
  16. J-Flash: Connecting to legacy ST STR912 devices failed. Fixed.
  17. J-Flash: From now, we output the CRC of the data file on open in the log window of J-Flash.
  18. Firmware: Added built-in HSS support to allow sampling frequencies of 1 kHz instead of 50 Hz.
    19. Affected firmwares: JLink-OB-SAM3U128
    JLink-OB-SAM3U128 V3

Version V6.16g (2017-07-10)

  1. DLL Updater: Added SEGGER Embedded Studio.

  6. DLL: Device selection dialog was not created as topmost window and therefore could be covered by the application's window if opened from within an IDE etc. Fixed.
  7. DLL: Having multiple WriteMem accesses to flash with ReadMem accesses to RAM etc. between them could cause following WriteMem accesses to not trigger further flash downloads. Fixed.
  8. DLL: NXP Kinetis K32W: Device names were incorrect. Fixed.
  9. DLL: ST STM32F3 series: We do no longer perform the RAM initialization as according to the manual, the STM32F3 series does not come with ECC RAM.
  10. DLL: When using command string "SetRestartOnClose = 0", some DLL internal caches were not invalidated and freed correctly, on close. Which could cause problems the next time, the DLL was opened. Fixed.
  11. Firmware: J-Trace PRO: Added support for ARMv8-M architecture.
  12. GDB Server: Corrected spelling mistakes in log output.
  13. J-Flash SPI: The application returned O.K. (0) instead of error (!= 0) in case of an incorrect data / project file has been passed via command line option. Fixed.
  14. J-Flash: "-open" command line option did not work when the specified path contained spaces. Fixed.
  15. TI CCS Plugin / Installer: Naming of plugin DLL/lib was inconsistent between Windows/Linux/Mac which has caused problems under some Linux installations. Fixed.
  16. TI CCS Plugin / Installer: Some J-Link script files threw syntax errors. Introduced with V6.16. Fixed.
  17. DLL: Data breakpoints (also called data events or watchpoints) could not be set while the CPU was running, even if the architecture allowed it (e.g. Cortex-M). Fixed.
  18. DLL: TI MSP432P401M / MSP432P401R: It seems like executing the flash algorithm (RAMCode) at 0x20000000 does not work. From now, we use the SRAM at 0x01000000. Fixed.
  19. DLL Updater: Added SEGGER Embedded Studio.
  20. Firmware: J-Link did not work properly if USB isolator was connected in between. Fixed.
    Affected firmwares: J-Link ULTRA+ V4
    J-Link PRO V4

Version V6.14h (2017-05-10)

  1. J-Flash stalled during creation of stand-alone mode data files when the flash features different sector sizes in one continuous range and certain conditions were met. Introduced with 6.14c / 6.15a. Fixed.
  2. RTTViewer: RTTViewer tried to read RTT data while handling error messages from the DLL. Fixed.
  3. RTTViewer: RTTViewer closed itself, if an error message was received from the DLL. Fixed.

Version V6.14g (2017-05-09)

  1. Commander: Commands "testnrspeed" and "testnwspeed" could end up in an endless loop with some combinations of and . Fixed.
  2. DLL (Linux): When running a Linux VM on a Mac host, connecting to J-Link could take considerably longer (about half a second) than in V6.12 series versions. Fixed.
  3. DLL (Mac): When running a Mac VM on a Mac host, connecting to J-Link could take considerably longer (about half a second) than in V6.12 series versions. Fixed.
  4. DLL: Analog Devices ADuCM331: Improved the flash algorithm so it is able to handle the temporary write protection (through the FEEPROP register).
  5. DLL: Analog Devices ADuCM331: Under special circumstances, flash algorithm did not return an error if erase failed due to active write protection. Fixed.
  6. DLL: Improved behavior for legacy ARM7 devices that need an initial reset pin toggle before debug interface gets responsive.
  7. DLL: J-Trace PRO for Cortex-M: Having multiple sessions with J-Trace PRO running in parallel and streaming via IP, did not work properly (local port allocation issue on PC side). Fixed.
  8. DLL: J-Trace PRO for Cortex-M: Streaming trace via IP did not work properly from inside VM via network adapters configured as NAT. Fixed.
  9. DLL: Some ADSP-CM41... target names did not work. Fixed.
  10. GDB Server: "JTAGConf" command line option did not support negative values which are required to configure auto-detect. Fixed.
  11. GDB Server: Added new command line option "jlinkscriptfile" which behaves similar to "scriptfile" (deprecated).
  12. Linux packages: Fixed 99-jlink.rules line-endings .

  2. DLL (SDK): JLINKARM_FindBP() did not work properly if there was a to-be-cleared soft breakpoint at a given address and a newly set hardware-breakpoint at the same address. Fixed.

  5. DLL: JLINKARM_EMU_GetDeviceInfo() did not return device info for the selected device if called with iEmu 0xFFFFFFFF. Fixed.
  6. DLL: NXP LPC824M201 could not be selected as target device. Introduced in V6.12c. Fixed.
  7. DLL: Implemented command string "SetRTTStreamingMode" to allow to block certain RTT read accesses from certain callers (e.g. to block read accesses via DLL API and only allow TELNET read accesses)
  8. DLLUpdater: 64-bit installations of Ozone were not found. Fixed.
  9. DLLUpdater: When updating 64-bit installation of supported IDEs, it could happen that a "sJLinkDevices.xml" file (note the 's' at the beginning) was created by accident (no negative side effects). Fixed.
  10. GDBServer: RTOS plug-in were not found under Linux, if the executable has been started using PATH environment variable. Fixed.
  11. J-Flash: In command-line mode, information message boxes of the J-Link DLL were not omitted. Fixed.
  12. J-Link Commander: Under certain conditions, swospeed displayed an invalid value if the connection to J-Link failed. Fixed.
  13. Firmware (Flasher): Under special circumstances a configuration conflict between secure and public area was reported, even if it was not the case. Fixed.
    Affected firmwares: Flasher ARM V4, Flasher PRO V4, Flasher Portable, Flasher PPC V4, Flasher RX V4
  14. Firmware: Added support for VMSD (basis for drag & drop programming support)
    Affected firmwares: J-Link BASE V10, J-Link PLUS V10, J-Link ULTRA+ V4, J-Link PRO V4, J-Link EDU V10
  15. Firmware: OpenSDA: Under very special circumstances it could happen that when sending data to the target via VCOM, the second byte sent after powering up OpenSDA was swallowed. Fixed.
    New firmware images: https://www.segger.com/downloads/jlink#JLinkOpenSDABoardSpecificFirmwares

Version V6.12d (2016-12-21)

  1. Firmware: J-Link did not work properly when long JTAG sequences (> 255 bytes) were output at once. Mainly happens when using legacy ARM 7/9 targets. Introduced with V6.12c. Fixed
    Affected firmwares: J-Link PRO V4, J-Link ULTRA+ V4
  2. DLL: Connecting to TI AM1705 devices could fail with error "Cannot find ICE-Pick (IDCODE mismatch)" even though the IDCODE was read correctly. Fixed.
  3. DLL: Control panel, RTT tab: Added possibility to send CR + LF on when sending RTT data to target
  4. J-Link RTT Viewer: Now remembers the 5 most recent devices name used.
  5. J-Link RTT Viewer: While in "Send on Enter" mode, RTT Viewer now has "command-line-like" history
  6. Firmware: Tx-Idle level for UART, used for virtual COM port, was LOW instead of HIGH which could cause problems when using VCOM. Fixed.
    Affected firmwares: ST-LINK OB V2 (available via latest STLinkReflash utility from SEGGER download area)
    ST-LINK OB V2-1 (available via latest STLinkReflash utility from SEGGER download area)
  7. DLL: When using "MRU device list" feature of J-Link SW (as for example RTTViewer does), getting the list of the most recently used device names could fail if called after a connection to J-Link was closed before. Fixed.

Version V6.12a (2016-12-02)

  1. Affected firmwares: J-Link V9, J-Link V10, J-Link ULTRA+ V4, J-Link PRO V4, J-Trace PRO V1 Cortex-M
  2. DLL (SDK): JLINKARM_EMU_GetList() sometimes counted J-Links connected via IP twice. Fixed.
  3. DLL (SDK): JLINKARM_EMU_GetList() under macOS and Linux did not return the total number of emulators which had been found if this number was bigger than MaxInfos. Fixed.
  4. DLL/J-Flash: Wrong function was used for chip erase. Fixed.

  6. DLL: Renesas RZ/T1: Under special circumstances, devices which were locked via an IDCODE were not detected as locked properly, so no authentication was performed, resulting in a non-functional debug session. Fixed.
  7. DLL: When connecting to a Renesas R5F52306 (RX230), an "unknown sub-family" warning was thrown. Fixed.
  8. Firmware: J-Link V10: When a connection to J-Link was opened, with no target connection requested, J-Link started driving the pins of the target interface. Fixed.
  9. Firmware: J-Link V9: When a connection to J-Link was opened, with no target connection requested, J-Link started driving the pins of the target interface. Fixed.
  10. Firmware: Under special circumstances HSS did not return an error if total number of bytes, to be sampled periodically, exceeded the buffer capacities of J-Link. Fixed.
  11. SWO Viewer: Added command line switches "-usb " and "-ip " which allows to configure the host interface.

Version V6.12 (2016-11-25)

  1. DLL (Linux): Connecting to EDBG, running J-Link OB firmware, did not work properly. Fixed.
  2. DLL (macOS): Connecting to EDBG, running J-Link OB firmware, did not work properly. Fixed.
  3. DLL: Added new script file variable "JLINK_AllowFlashCacheState" which can be used to enable / disable the flash cache.
  4. DLL: Added official names for ARM v8M Baseline and Mainline: Cortex-M23 and Cortex-M33.
  5. DLL: Added official names for ARM v8M Baseline and Mainline: Cortex-M23 and Cortex-M33.
  6. DLL: Added support for NXP iMX6UL series devices.
  7. DLL: Added support for ST STM32H7 series devices.
  8. DLL: Changed unsecure message box warning text for nRF51.
  9. DLL: Flash programming did not work for Silicon Labs EFR32MG series devices. Fixed.
  10. DLL: For multi-bank devices the flash area information was not created when requesting the device info. Fixed.
  11. DLL: If CPU was reset while SWO running, the device specific initialization was not performed again. Fixed.
  12. DLL: Removed secured device detection for Nordic Semi nRF51 series devices.
  13. DLL: SWO device specific initialization für LPC5411x was not correct. Fixed.
  14. DLL: Under special circumstances, flash programming did not work for SAMG55 series devices. Fixed.
  15. DLL: Under very rare circumstances, when setting/clearing breakpoints while the CPU was running, the CPU was halted even if not necessary (e.g. clearing hardware breakpoints only and the CPU supports this during program execution)
  16. DLL: When clearing breakpoint after the connection to the CPU was lost (low power state, target disconnected due to bad cable etc.), it could happen that the J-Link software ended up in an endless recursion. Fixed.
  17. DLL: When doing instruction single stepping with streaming trace enabled, it could happen that trace was not restarted correctly after a few steps. Fixed.
  18. GDB Server: Added additional error checks for "qSeggerSWO:*" commands, added info to these commands to the manual.
  19. GDB Server: Added new command line argument "-listprobes " which can be used to get a list of all connected J-Link debug probes.
  20. GDB Server: Added new command line argument "-powertarget " which can be used to enable the J-Link supply voltage via Pin19 to power the target.
  21. GDB Server: SWO analyzer could crash under special circumstances. Fixed.
  22. J-Flash/DLL: Added PCodes to JLINKARM_DEVICE_GetInfo().
  23. J-Flash: Added error message if not all data could be programmed.
  24. J-Flash: Added log outputs for each saved/downloaded PCode file.
  25. J-Flash: Added option to disable flash banks.
  26. J-Flash: Added reference project file for nRF51822 devices which unlocks the device in the Init steps.
  27. J-Flash: Changed the main menu structure.
  28. J-Flash: Changed the production tab options.
  29. J-Flash: disabled flash banks should not disable the check if selected data fits into the sectors selected.
  30. J-Link Commander: Updated testnrspeed / testnwspeed commands to accept transfer sizes up to 64 KB per loop.

Version V6.12n (2016-11-18)

  1. DLL (SDK): Added SPI API description + samples to the J-Link SDK user manual.
  2. DLL (SDK): Added the x64 bit versions of the J-Link libraries.
  3. DLL (SDK): Calls of JLINKARM_DEVICE_GetIndex() were not thread-safe. Which could cause problems when another thread was calling JLINKARM_Close() in parallel. Fixed.
  4. DLL (SDK): Calls of JLINKARM_DEVICE_GetInfo() were not thread-safe. Which could cause problems when another thread was calling JLINKARM_Close() in parallel. Fixed.
  5. DLL: Added QSPI flash programming support for Renesas RZ/A1LU series devices (R7S721030, R7S721031 and R7S721034).
  6. DLL: Added debug support for TI CC3200 series
  7. DLL: Added flash programming support for Silicon Labs EZR32HG220F32, EZR32HG220F64, EZR32HG320F32 and EZR32HG320F64 series devices.
  8. DLL: Added new script file function to override the reset type used by the J-Link DLL in case of reset is issued.
  9. DLL: Added official names for ARM v8M Baseline and Mainline: Cortex-M23 and Cortex-M33.
  10. DLL: Added two new J-Link script file functions which are executed right after and before flash programming (e.g. initial flash download or flash breakpoints): HandleBeforeFlashProg() and HandleAfterFlashProg()
  11. DLL: Added unsecure for nRF51.
  12. DLL: Cortex-M: When using backtrace over small code regions (backtrace between 2 breakpoints which have a few subroutines between them), it could happen that an empty list or a list full of addr. 0xFFFFFFF0 was shown (e.g. in Ozone). Fixed.
  13. DLL: Improved trace start/stop setup performance
  14. DLL: In case an error occurred during streaming trace, error messages were not output in a thread-safe way which could cause problems in some environments
  15. DLL: J-Trace PRO Cortex-M V1: Instruction trace in IAR EWARM and Keil uVision did not work correctly (no trace data was shown in instruction trace window). Fixed.
  16. DLL: Under special circumstances, R7FS5D97 devices were configured incorrectly during restore after a download to flash memory. Fixed.
  17. DLL: Under special circumstances, flash programming did not work for NXP (Freescale) KL82 series devices. Fixed.
  18. DLL: Under special circumstances, reset did not work properly for ADuCM350 series devices. Fixed.
  19. Firmware OB-SAM3U128-NordicSemi: Mass erase could not be performed, if device was protected with protection level PALL. Fixed.
  20. J-Flash SPI: CRC on data file open was not calculated correctly. Fixed.
  21. J-Flash: Added QSPI flash programming support for Renesas RZ/A1LU series devices (R7S721030, R7S721031 and R7S721034).
  22. J-Flash: Added flash programming support for Silicon Labs EZR32HG220F32, EZR32HG220F64, EZR32HG320F32 and EZR32HG320F64 series devices.
  23. RemoteServer: Switched to SYS functions.
  24. RemoteServer: UDP thread did not terminate on some Linux distributions. Fixed.

  8. DLL: In case the application did not set an external handler for warning outputs, these messages were swallowed. Fixed.
  9. DLL: STRACE could cause an access violation used on cores where STRACE is not supported (e.g. ARM7/9). Fixed.

  12. DLL: When accessing the same J-Link with multiple processes without explicitly selecting the J-Link via its S/N (through the API), an internal error indicating that the USB communication is not locked, could pop-up. Introduced in V6.10k. Fixed.
  13. Firmware: J-Trace PRO Cortex-M V1: Under special circumstances J-Link software reported unknown trace packets when trace data load was high. Fixed.
  14. Firmware: J-Trace PRO Cortex-M V1: When streaming much trace data via IP (>= 80 MB/s) for a longer period of time (> 2 h), under special circumstances the IP interface of J-Trace could become unresponsive. Fixed.

Version V6.10i (2016-10-25)

  1. DLL: Added some missing Silicon Labs EFM8 devices.
  2. DLL: CFI flash programming (Intel based algorithms) did not work for Cortex-AR devices. Fixed.
  3. DLL: CFI flash programming did not work for Cortex-M7 series devices. Fixed.
  4. DLL: Under special circumstances, DEMCR.TRCENA was not cleared on debug session close. Fixed.
  5. DLL: Under special circumstances, DHCSR.C_DEBUGEN was not cleared on debug session close. Fixed.
  6. DLL: Windows: Under special circumstances, when heavily creating and closing processes that connect to multiple J-Links connected to the same PC, it could happen that internal lock count errors occur. Fixed.
  7. DLL: macOS: When multiple processes accessed the same J-Link, under special circumstances accesses were not serialized correctly, resulting in incorrect behavior / failure. Fixed.
  8. Flasher: Stand-alone mode programming of Atmel SAMD20 devices did not work when the data image included option bytes (fuses). Fixed.
  9. GDBServer: Some targets could put into a state where a connect succeeds but halting the CPU fails (CPU does not respond to debug halt request) and this behavior could be cured by a reset. This has been seen on some Cortex-M devices.
    The failed halt request made GDBServer to return with an error immediately, instead of trying to "cure" this state via reset. Fixed.
  10. J-Flash: "Chip erase" did not work for SPIFI flash banks (e.g. RZ/A1H). Fixed.
  11. J-Flash: Under special circumstances, the -saveas command line argument did not work properly. Fixed.

  2. DLL: Connecting to Cortex-M targets via JTAG could fail (SWD was not affected), in case there is buggy silicon that implements incorrect ROM tables. Fixed.
  3. DLL: Some Silicon Labs EFM8 derivative names passed bei Keil PK51 were reported as unknown device names. Fixed.
  4. J-Flash: Flash programming in stand-alone mode could fail under special circumstance. Introduced in V6.10b. Fixed.

Version V6.10e (2016-10-14)

  1. DLL (SDK): Not all Coprocessor instructions, and Supervisor Call have been disassembled correctly. Fixed.
  2. DLL: Added generic debug support for Vorago PA32KAS, VA10800 and VA10820 series devices.
