  4. DLL: Added new exec command which allows to specify a J-Link log file.
  5. DLL: Connecting to TI OMAP5910 failed. Fixed.
  6. DLL: Connecting to TI OMAP5912 failed. Fixed.
  7. DLL: J-Trace PRO Cortex-M: When not having Ethernet connected, it could take up to 2 seconds until streaming trace via USB was started. Fixed.
  8. DLL: Linux: Having multiple processes accessing the same J-Link at the same time did not work (second process failed to open a connection to J-Link). Fixed.
  9. DLL: Linux: Under some Linux distributions it could crash on debug session start when used with SEGGER Embedded Studio. The J-Link lib did not exit a thread gracefully. Fixed.
  10. DLL: Silicon Labs J-Link OB on old EFM32-DK boards: Under special circumstances it could happen, that the J-Link OB firmware hang at debug session start, after flash download. Fixed.
  11. DLL: Some Renesas RXv1 targets (e.g. RX111) could not be programmed correctly and threw errors. Introduced in V5.10i. Fixed.
  12. DLL: Under special circumstances a deadlock could occur when multiple processes accessed the same J-Link and target and one of the processes was IAR EWARM and the target was a Cortex-M device accessed via SWD. Fixed.
  13. DLL: Under special circumstances, reset strategy "core only" for Cortex-M devices did not work correctly when using the JTAG interface (SWD worked fine). Fixed.
  14. DLL: Updated NXP LPC5460x device names.
  15. Flasher: Stand-alone mode programming of secured NXP (Freescale) SKEAZ devices did not work. Fixed.
  16. J-Flash: When using "Chip" as erase option with AUTO, under curtain conditions, only the selected sectors were erased. Fixed.
  17. Software Package: Added JTAG Load to the macOS and Linux packages.
  18. Software Package: We do no longer zip the setup executable files for windows but provide the setup executables directly.

Version V6.10d (2016-10-06)

  1. DLL (SDK): Introduced special error codes for STRACE_Read(): In case something went wrong during the analysis and we do not know the exact PC, 0xFFFFFFF0 - 0xFFFFFFFF will be returned as address for the executed instruction, in the list of executed instructions.
  2. DLL (SDK): It is no longer necessary to explicitly call STRACE_Stop() before reading STRACE data.
  3. DLL (SDK): Sample_RAWTRACE.c did throw warnings under Linux/Mac. Fixed.
  4. DLL: Disassembly of data processing instructions and MSR did not process the immediate value correctly. Fixed.
  5. DLL: Linux/Mac: One USB thread was not terminated correctly on debug session close (no side effects so far). Fixed.
  6. DLL: Linux/Mac: Some threads were not terminated correctly which could cause a hang of the DLL on debug session close. Fixed.
  7. DLL: Linux/Mac: Streaming trace could crash on debug session close (possible NULL pointer dereference under special circumstances). Fixed.
  8. DLL: Mac: Streaming trace via IP did not work because failing to configure the receive buffer size on MacOS was treated as an error. Fixed.
  9. DLL: Silicon Labs EFM8 series: Connect could fail with Silicon Labs on-board J-Link (external J-Links work fine). Introduced in V6.10a. Fixed.
  10. DLL: Streaming trace could hang if more than 2 network adapters were installed on the PC. Fixed.
  11. DLL: Webserver thread was not terminated properly on debug session close (no side effects so far). Fixed.
  12. J-Flash: Some uncommon mot file generators used lower case characters a-f for data + address in mot files, which could throw a checksum error in J-Flash. Fixed.
  13. J-Link Commander: Changed default speed for C2 target interface (used by Silicon Labs EFM8 series) to 1 MHz as 4 MHz are too much for most eval boards.
  14. J-Link Commander: Default speed for FINE connections is now 1000 kHz instead of 4000 kHz.

Version V6.10c (2016-09-28)

  1. DLL: STM32L4 series devices with single bank were not handled correctly. Fixed.
  2. DLL: EEPROM size and RAM size for some ST STM32Lxxx devices was incorrect. Fixed.
  3. J-Flash: CFI flash always used 1kB buffers for programming which led to poor programming performance. Fixed.
  4. J-Flash/Firmware: Return value of _IsBlankUseRAM() was not checked. Fixed.
  5. Firmware: Added error messages from flash module to console output.
  6. Firmware: Added HWINFO about IP configuration.
    Affected firmwares: Flasher ARM V4
    Flasher PRO V4
    Flasher RX V4
    Flasher PPC V4
    Flasher Portable V1
  7. Firmware: Under special circumstances, verify via readback could fail in stand-alone mode. Fixed.
  8. DLL (SDK): If JLink.lib was used by a DLL, not directly by a executable, auto-loading of a JLinkARM.dll in the same directory as the DLL that included JLink.lib did not work correctly. Fixed.
    9. Sample case that did not work:
    Executable: C:\MyProg\bin\MyProg.exe
    DLL that includes JLink.lib and uses the J-Link DLL: C:\MyProg\DLLs\MyDLL.dll
    Location of JLinkARM.dll: C:\MyProg\DLLs\JLinkARM.dll <- JLink.lib tried to load JLinkARM.dll from C:\MyProg\bin

Version V6.10b (2016-09-26)

  1. J-Flash: Overlapping memory areas were not always detected while reading *.mot files. Fixed.
  2. J-Flash: Project files got corrupted if no sectors for a flash bank were selected. Fixed.
  3. J-Flash: Stand-alone mode did not work for Infineon TLE98xx series devices. Fixed.
  4. DLL: Under special circumstances, flash programming did not work for Infineon XMC4500 series devices (erase timeout). Fixed.
  5. DLL: Added single stepping workaround for buggy Cortex-M7 r0p0 and r0p1 devices (e.g. ST STM32F74xxx and STM32F75xxx series), so PC does not accidentally end up in ISR on single stepping.
  6. DLL: When having a n NXP LPCXpresso-OB or LPC-Link2 (running J-Link firmware) connected, all speed selections below 4 MHz resulted in 4 MHz being selected. Fixed.
  7. DLL: When quickly opening + closing multiple instances of the DLL in parallel, each connecting to a separate J-Link, it could happen that a "Could not connect to J-Link" error was thrown. Fixed.

Version V6.00e (2016-08-04)

  1. Firmware: HSS sampling was not immediately paused when the target halted. Fixed.
    Affected firmwares: J-Link V9
    J-Link V10
    J-Link ULTRA+ V4
    J-Link PRO V4
    J-Trace PRO V1 Cortex-M
  2. DLL: Under special circumstances, the RAM usage calculation did not calculate the optimum amount of RAM for SPIFI flash programming. Introduced in V6.00. Fixed.
  3. DLL: Under special circumstances, the incorrect verify method has been used resulting in longer verify times. Introduced in V6.00. Fixed.
  4. DLL: Under special circumstances, the J-Link DLL erroneously reported "Emulator does not support RAWTRACE.". Fixed.
  5. DLL: STM32F2xx, STM32F4xx, STM32F7xx series devices: During the unlock procedure, Bits [11:08] of nWRP of the 1st flash bank were not reset to factory default. Fixed.
  6. DLL: STM32F469xx, STM32F479xx series devices: During the unlock procedure, SPRMOD and nWRP of the 2nd flash bank were not reset to factory default. Fixed.
  7. J-Link STM32 Unlock utility: STM32F2xx, STM32F4xx, STM32F7xx series devices: During the unlock procedure, Bits [11:08] of nWRP of the 1st flash bank were not reset to factory default. Fixed.
  8. J-Link STM32 Unlock utility: STM32F469xx, STM32F479xx series devices: During the unlock procedure, SPRMOD and nWRP of the 2nd flash bank were not reset to factory default. Fixed.
  9. J-Link STM32 Unlock utility: Added support for STM32F76xxx and STM32F77xxx series devices.
  10. DLL/Firmware: HSS was not temporarily stopped during flash programming which could result in garbage values being read in case a flash download occurred while HSS was active/running. Fixed
  11. J-Link Commander: When changing the target interface when already being connected to a target via another target interface, new interface was not selected immediately but on next command. Fixed.
  12. DLL: ST STM32F77xxx: Auto-detection of RTT control block did not work if it was in address range 0x20000000 - 0x2000FFFF. Fixed.
  13. DLL: Cortex-M: Under special circumstances the log "Debugger tries to set PC to odd value..." was output by the DLL when used with some debuggers (e.g. SEGGER Ozone), even though everything was O.K. Fixed.
  14. DLL: HSS data was still requested from J-Link even if the target CPU was not running, resulting in unnecessary CPU load on DLL side while there was no activity on the target side. Improved.
  15. DLL: HSS timestamp was not "halted" while target CPU was halted, resulting in non-continuous timestamps in case CPU was halted + started multiple times, which could look like data was lost (due to buffer overflows etc.) even in case no data was lost. Fixed.
  16. DLL: Changed STM32 unlock behavior: Where possible, the DLL now only resets the Option Bytes that effect the Read/Write protection status of the device (the User Option Bytes stay untouched). If a complete reset to factory defaults of the Option Bytes is desired, the J-Link STM32 Unlock utility (JLinkSTM32.exe) can be used. Therefore, the J-Link DLL no longer resets the User Option Bytes of the following device series: STM32L0xx, STM32L1xx, STM32L4xx , STM32F0xx, STM32F1xx, STM32F3xx
  17. Firmware: RTT: Improved error handling in case target entered a low power mode that inhibited J-Link from reading RAM contents
    Affected firmwares: J-Link V9
    J-Link V10
    J-Link ULTRA+ V4
    J-Link PRO V4
    J-Trace PRO V1 Cortex-M
    ST-LINK V2
    ST-LINK V2-1
  18. DLL: When connecting with multiple processes to the same J-Link in parallel, using different target interface speeds in each process, the processes could hang. Fixed.

  9. DLL: Silicon Labs EFM8 series devices: Under special circumstances, it could happen that high-level (C-source) stepping in the IDE did not work correctly. Fixed.

  1. DLL: Flash Programming did not work properly on Analog Devices ADucM360 devices. Fixed.

  5. DLL: Connect under reset did not work properly for ST STM32L4 series devices. Fixed.
  6. DLL: Monitor mode support added in V5.02 could cause compatibility problems with Rowley CrossWorks IDE and ARM7/9 devices. Fixed.
  7. DLL: Connecting to Freescale Kinetis V5x series devices (Cortex-M7) could cause an error message "Communication error while accessing AHB-AP". Fixed.
  8. DLL: Some STM32 device names in Keil MDK-ARM were not recognized correctly. Fixed.
  9. DLL: Read protection check did not work reliable for STM32 devices if core is in sleep mode. Fixed.
  10. DLL: Unnecessary reset has been performed during connect on Atmel SAMD & SAML series devices. Fixed.
  11. DLL: The RX ID code verification edit field did not allow scrolling. Fixed.
  12. Firmware: Flasher Portable: Under special circumstances, the SPI target interface did not work properly. Fixed.
  13. Firmware: Flasher V3: Under special circumstances, the Flasher erased the EEPROM in stand-alone mode, even if it was not selected. Fixed.
  14. J-Flash: Renesas Synergy R7FS7G2 devices were missing. Fixed.
  15. J-Flash: Renesas Synergy R7FS3A7 devices were missing. Fixed.
  16. J-Flash: Renesas Synergy R7FS124 devices were missing. Fixed.
  17. DLL: Enhanced functionality of JLINKARM_GetDebugInfo() function.
  18. DLL (SDK): Doc: Prototype of JLINK_DownloadFile() corrected.
  19. DLL: Renamed STR9 "Bootbank: 1" device selections to "Bootbank 1"
  20. J-Flash: Renamed STR9 "Bootbank: 1" device selections to "Bootbank 1"
  21. DLL (Linux): In case multiple J-Links were connected to the same PC, an error message that no connection at all could be established, was thrown. As long as dialogs are not available under Linux, the DLL will connect to the first J-Link found.
  22. DLL (OS X): In case multiple J-Links were connected to the same PC, an error message that no connection at all could be established, was thrown. As long as dialogs are not available under OS X, the DLL will connect to the first J-Link found.

  7. Firmware: Flasher: The ASCII interface command "Select" did not work properly. Fixed.
  8. Firmware: Flasher: Flash programming did not work properly if multiple flash banks were used. Fixed.
  9. Firmware: Flasher: Under special circumstances, blank check operation failed in stand-alone mode even though no error happened. Fixed.
  10. DLL: TELNET channel provided by DLL was closed if character 0x03 was received via RTT. Fixed.
  11. DLL: Added firmware for J-Link-OB-MB9AF312K-Spansion.
  12. DLL: Added support for NordicSemi nRF52 series devices.
  13. J-Flash: Added command line options "-setrxidcode" to allow setting of IDCODE to allow connecting to protected RX targets.
  14. DLL: Added alias for Freescale WPR1516: Now also the device name "WPR1516M2" is accepted.

Version 5.00c (2015-06-11)

  1. DLL/J-Flash: Selecting an ST STM32F427xI / STM32F429xI device could cause an internal error of type MEM_MAP_AddRegion() or an memory allocation error. Fixed. Other STM series were not affected by this problem.
  2. DLL/J-Flash: Selecting a Renesas R5F51104, R5F51114 or R5F564MF lead to the error message "MEM_MAP_AddRegion Function called with start address greater than end address". Fixed. Other devices were not affected by this problem.
  3. DLL/J-Flash: Selecting a SiLabs SiM3C, SiM3L or SiM3U series device, could lead to the error message "Buffer overflow in memory block (1 bytes overflowed)" . Fixed. Other device series were not affected by this problem.
  4. DLL/J-Flash: Selecting the NXP PCF87750 as device could lead to a misleading error message regarding a pointer being invalid. Fixed. Other devices were not affected by this problem.
  5. J-Flash: Sectorization of Renesas R5F51104, R5F51114 and R5F564MF was incorrect. Fixed.
  6. J-Flash: Device ID for R5F56318 devices was incorrect. Corrected.

Version 5.00b (2015-06-10)

  1. DLL: Exec SetRXIDCode did not work properly. Fixed.
  2. DLL: QSPI flash programming: Improved read speed on Renesas RZ devices.
  3. DLL: QSPI flash programming: Macronix flash devices were not handled correctly. Fixed.
  4. DLL: Flash programming for flashes > 1 MB could fail (e.g. STM32F429 series was affected by this). Introduced in V5.00 with QSPI flash support. Fixed.
  5. DLL: Renesas RX via FINE: Auto-enable of ongoing debug mode (caused flash programming internally) could fail. Introduced in V5.00 with QSPI flash support. Fixed.
  6. DLL: Renesas RX R5F56138 devices with ID 0x0D018447 were detected incorrectly. Fixed.
  7. J-Flash/DLL: Under special circumstances, flash programming of Analog Devices ADuCM350 did not work properly. Fixed.

Version 5.00a (2015-06-09)

  1. J-Flash/DLL: When performing a reset on an empty Kinetis K-series device, subsequent flash programming could fail. Introduced in V5.00 (when performing changes to support a new derivative from the V-series). Fixed.

Version 4.98d

  1. DLL: If a flash sector was only half-way erased but read as empty by the CPU, programming errors could occur during flash download (Mainly seen on Infineon XMC series CPUs). Fixed.

  4. DLL/J-Flash: Added flash programming support for Nuvoton NUC029L series.
  5. DLL: The watchdog of Kinetis L-series devices has been disabled by the DLL on connect. We removed this behavior and make sure that the watchdog will be fed when enabled.

  48. Firmware: J-Link PRO: Under special circumstances, communication via IP broke down if J-Link and host PC are in different subnets. Fixed.
  49. Firmware: Flasher ARM V4: Explicit control of pin 9 via JLINKARM_SetTCK() / JLINKARM_ClrTCK() did not work properly. Fixed.
  50. Firmware: J-Link-Lite-XMC4200: Under special circumstances, JTAG/SWD communication problems could occur on some eval boards. Fixed.
  51. Firmware: J-Link-Lite-XMC4200: Wrong target interface speed reported by firmware (actual speed was higher than reported one). Fixed.
  52. Firmware: J-Link V9: nTRST pin was not set as input of J-Link if SWD was used as target interfaced.
    53. It could cause problems if nTRST was shared with GPIO functionality on the target hardware and pin was connected to J-Link. Fixed.
  53. DLL: Under special circumstances, debugging on ARM7/9 S-cores (e.g. ARM926EJ-S) and older IAR EWARM versions could fail. Problem introduced in V4.80 of the J-Link DLL. Fixed.
  54. DLL: In case of programming errors, flash cache of DLL was not invalidated correctly. Fixed.
  55. DLL: Under special circumstances, if using old IAR EWARM versions, the error message "DLL function JLINKARM_SetFlashArea(...)" not found, could appear. Fixed.
  56. DLL: Under special circumstances, the error message "MEM_MAP.c, _LogRange2PhysRange()..." could appear. Fixed.
  57. DLL: Under special circumstances, speed set by debugger was not configured correctly on J-Link which could cause problems on some targets. Introduced in V4.80a. Fixed.
  58. DLL: ARM7/9 targets: Under special circumstances when single stepping a MOVS PC, LR (return from exception), instruction set simulation did not work properly. Fixed.
  59. DLL: Under very special circumstances when reading memory areas where software breakpoints were set and flash cache was disabled, incorrect memory contents could be shown. Fixed.
  60. DLL: Atmel SAM4L: Under special circumstances, CYCCNT was not incremented on Go/Continue. Fixed.
  61. DLL: Some device names passed by IAR EWARM for ADI ADSP-CM40x series devices (Cortex-M4) were not recognized correctly. Fixed.
  62. DLL: Cortex-M: CycleCnt was not updated on single stepping. Fixed.
  63. DLL: AM3359: Reset did not halt CPU at start of public ROM code. Fixed.
  64. DLL: Flash programming for Microsemi SmartFusion2 series devices did not work properly. Fixed.
  65. DLL: Under special circumstances, on some devices when writing to aliased memory areas (e.g. cached-flash range vs. non-cached range) and immediately reading from them, incorrect memory contents were displayed. Fixed.
  66. DLL: PIC32: Physical addresses for internal flash were not mapped correctly during flash programming. Fixed.
  67. DLL: Cypress PSoC4: Under special circumstances CPU could get stuck when using software breakpoints in flash memory. Fixed.
  68. DLL: Atmel SAM3U series: Under special circumstances, flash download to address 0x0 did not work properly, since memory mapping was not handled properly. Fixed.
  69. DLL: Some device names passed by IAR EWARM were not handled correctly. Fixed.
  70. DLL: Cirrus Logic EP7312 was reported as ARM9 while it is an ARM7 device. Fixed.
  71. DLL: SWOViewer did not work properly for STM32L devices. Fixed.
  72. DLL: Cortex-M: Writing the CONTROL register in Freescale CodeWarrior did not work properly. Fixed.
  73. DLL: Under special circumstances on devices with multiple RAM areas, PUSH/POP instruction was not simulated properly when using instruction set simulation. Fixed.
  74. DLL: When selecting a device via "device ?" in J-Link Commander, it was not possible to switch device selection to another device, without restarting J-Link Commander. Fixed.
  75. DLL (RX): Connecting to J-Link PRO via Ethernet when using HEW / EWRX was not possible. Fixed.
  76. DLL/RDI: Under special circumstances, an internal error could occur, saying "Invalid memory map, can not un-alias region 0x00000000 - 0xFFFFFFFF". Fixed.
  77. DLL/J-Flash: Under special circumstances flash secure/unsecure for ST STM32F3xx devices did not work properly. Fixed.
  78. DLL/J-Flash: If error occurred during erasing/programming the QSPI flash on Renesas RZ devices, error flags in flash status register were not reset correctly. Fixed.
  79. DLL/J-Flash: Under special circumstances, flash programming on Fujitsu/Spansion FM0+ devices did not work properly. Fixed.
  80. DLL/J-Flash: Under special circumstances, unlimited flash breakpoints feature did not work properly on Fujitsu/Spansion FM0+ series devices. Fixed.
  81. DLL/J-Flash: Incorrect RAM size has been reported for some ST STM32F105 / 107 devices. Fixed.
  82. DLL/J-Flash: Freescale Kinetis V series devices: When inhibiting accidental secure of a device during flash programming, incorrect byte at address 0x40E was modified, instead of byte at address 0x40C. Fixed.
  83. J-Flash: Open last data file did not work properly. Fixed.
  84. J-Flash: Last data file opened with a specific project was not opened automatically on startup. Fixed.
  85. J-Flash: -openprj command line option did not work properly. Fixed.
  86. J-Flash: If "power target via J-Link" was enabled in production settings and "Start application" was also enabled, "start application" could fail. Fixed.
  87. J-Flash: LPC43xx devices were listed as "Cortex-M3" instead of "Cortex-M4". Fixed.
  88. J-Flash: RAM base address in NordicSemi nRF51422.jflash example project was configured incorrectly. Fixed.
  89. J-Mem: When reading from addresses at memory boundaries, under special circumstances memory contents could not be displayed. Fixed.
  90. GDB Server: Under special circumstances unhandled exception could occur when closing GDBServer while target CPU was running. Fixed.
  91. GDB Server: Starting multiple GDBServer instances from different users via SSH did not work properly. Fixed.
  92. GDB Server CL: Under some circumstances the output contained blank lines after each line. Fixed.
  93. DLL: J-Link script file no longer necessary when connecting to TI AM18xx target devices. Selecting the correct device is sufficient.
  94. DLL J-Link script file no longer necessary when connecting to TI OMAP-L138 target devices. Selecting the correct device is sufficient.
  95. DLL/J-Flash: STM32L: Programming speed of EEPROM area improved.
  96. DLL/J-Flash: Adapted new naming scheme of Nordic Semi devices.
  97. GDB Server CL: Do not save and load (GUI related) settings anymore.
  98. Software package: RDI manual UM08004_JLinkRDI.pdf has been merged into J-Link manual UM08001_JLink.pdf.
  99. J-Link User Guide: Several corrections / improvements.

  27. DLL/J-Flash: Flash programming for STM32F2xx / STM32F4xx devices could fail if device was running at <= 2.0V VCC. Fixed.
  28. DLL/SWOViewer: SWO did not work properly for Kinetis K-series devices. Fixed.
  29. DLL/GDBServer: DLL flash programming logic: When downloading large applications on STM32 devices to flash, via address 0x0, it could happen that flash programming failed if application size exceeded a specific value. Fixed.
  30. DLL: Cortex-M: Instruction set simulation caused problems if debugger accidentally set PC to an odd address. Fixed.
  31. DLL: Under special circumstances, when "auto" target interface speed was selected on ARM7/9 devices, accidentally "adaptive clocking" was selected, even if not supported by the connected core. Fixed.
  32. DLL: Under special circumstances, target power loss was not detected properly during flash programming. Fixed.
  33. DLL: Reset for Renesas RZ device did not work correctly if boot mode 3 (boot from QSPI flash) was selected. Fixed.
  34. DLL: Flash programming on nRF51422 devices could fail since non 4 KB aligned start address of nRF51422 RAM was not handled correctly. Fixed.
  35. DLL: Some Atmel SAM3/SAM4 devices were reported as unknown devices when using J-Link with EWARM. Fixed.
  36. DLL: Atmel ATSAMD20: If target application issued a reset during the debug session (via watchdog etc.), target application did not correctly reboot while J-Link was connected. Fixed.
  37. DLL (RX): RX630 / RX631 F-series devices where not detected properly, which could cause problems during debugging and flash programming in Renesas HEW / e2Studio and IAR EWRX.
  38. DLL (SDK): DLL exec "map region" did not work correctly. Fixed.
  39. DLL (SDK): If JLINKARM_ClrBPEx() was called after the CPU has been started via JLINKARM_Go() and before JLINKARM_IsHalted() was called and the CPU was halted in the meantime, it was possible that the CPU was accidentally started after the breakpoint was removed. Fixed.
  40. DLL (Linux): Under special circumstances, connection to J-Link V7 probes could fail. Fixed.
  41. DLL (Linux / MAC): When being connected to J-Link via IP and having longer idle times where no communication with J-Link was performed by the debugger, it could happen that the IP communication broke down. Fixed.
  42. J-Flash: If padding of programming data was necessary to achieve flash min. align requirements, data was always padded with 0xFF, even on flashes which have 0x00 as erased value, which caused verification errors. Fixed.
  43. J-Flash: Under special circumstances, "chip erase" for AT91SAM9XE devices failed. Fixed.
  44. J-Flash: Some Cortex-M4 target devices were listed as Cortex-M3. Fixed.
  45. J-Flash: Cortex-M4 devices accidentally were listed as Cortex-M3. Fixed.
  46. J-Flash: Energy Micro Zero Gecko Devices were listed as Cortex-M3 devices. Fixed.
  47. J-Flash: Fujitsu/Spansion FM4 series MCUs were listed as Cortex-M3 instead of Cortex-M4. Fixed.
  48. Firmware: Flasher Portable: Incorrect CFI information reported by some SST39 CFI NOR flash devices was not handled correctly in stand-alone mode. Fixed.
  49. Firmware: J-Link V8 / V9: When debugging on Cortex-M via SWD interface and using a very old DLL (< V4.10 from year 2009) debugging might fail due to a firmware <-> DLL incompatibility. Fixed.
  50. Firmware: Flasher (ARM/PPC/RX): Under special circumstances, switching the baudrate did not work properly. Fixed.
  51. Firmware: J-Link ULTRA V1, J-Link PRO V1: Under special circumstances, single stepping on Cortex-A/R devices did not work properly if D-cache was enabled. Fixed.
  52. Firmware: Flasher Portable: Stand-alone programming of RX6xx devices via JTAG did not work properly. Fixed.
  53. Firmware: Flasher ARM V4 / Flasher Portable: Under special circumstances, on recoverable NAND flash failure, Flasher did not allow further writing of the on board NAND flash (causing e.g. firmware updates to be rejected)
  54. Firmware: J-Link-OB-XMC4200: VCOM functionality did not work correctly when receiving data from target system. Fixed.
  55. Firmware: Flasher ARM V3: SetTCK/ClrTCK in J-Link Commander did not work properly. Fixed.
  56. GDBServer (Mac): Under special circumstances, a seg fault 11 could occur if a GDB-TCP/IP connection was closed. Fixed.
  57. GDBServer: Under special circumstances, when having more than 1 GDB connection open to GDB Server GDB commands got intermixed. Fixed.
  58. GDBServer: Semihosting: SYS_FLEN command did not work properly. Fixed.
  59. GDBServer: Semihosting: SYS_FCLOSE command did not work properly. Fixed. (Usually did not cause any real problems)
  60. J-Link manual: Several corrections in GDBServer section.
  61. Firmware: Boot-up time of J-Link ULTRA+/Pro V4 improved.
  62. DLL/J-Flash: Flash programming speed for Renesas RX200 devices improved (doubled).
  63. J-Flash: Some flash sectors were not selected in the sample projects of AT91SAM4S devices by default. Corrected.
